<script>
  // Script remains unchanged
  const details = document.querySelectorAll('.accordion-item');
  details.forEach(targetDetail => {
    targetDetail.addEventListener('click', () => {
      details.forEach(detail => {
        if (detail !== targetDetail) detail.removeAttribute('open');
      });
    });
  });
</script>

// --- CORRECTED: Restored author link using the new robust slugify function ---
import type { Locale } from '../i18n';
import { useTranslations } from '../lib/i18n';
import { createPath, slugify } from '../lib/paths';

export interface Props {
  title: string;
  publishedAt: string;
  author: string;
  tags?: string[];
  lang?: Locale;
}

const { title, publishedAt, author, tags = [], lang = 'en' } = Astro.props;
const t = useTranslations(lang);

const formattedDate = new Date(publishedAt).toLocaleDateString(lang === 'hi' ? 'hi-IN' : 'en-IN', {
  year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric'
});

// The author link is now restored and will work correctly for all languages
const authorUrl = createPath(`/blog/author/${slugify(author)}/`, lang);

const category = tags.length > 0 ? tags[0] : null;
const otherTags = tags.slice(1);
---
<header class="article-head">
  <div class="meta">
    {category && (
      <>
        <a href={createPath(`/blog/category/${slugify(category)}/`, lang)} class="category-pill">{category}</a>
        <span aria-hidden="true">•</span>
      </>
    )}
    <time datetime={publishedAt}>{formattedDate}</time>
    <span aria-hidden="true">•</span>
    {/* The author is a link again, with correct i18n formatting and URL */}
    <span>
      {t('blogPost.byAuthor').replace('{authorName}', '')}
      <a href={authorUrl} rel="author">{author}</a>
    </span>
  </div>

  <h1 class="title">{title}</h1>

  {otherTags.length > 0 && (
    <div class="tags" aria-label="Tags">
      {otherTags.map(tag => (
        <a href={createPath(`/blog/tag/${slugify(tag)}/`, lang)} class="tag">{tag}</a>
      ))}
    </div>
  )}
</header>
<style>
/* Styles are restored to support the link */

.meta a{color:var(--text-secondary);text-decoration:none;font-weight:600}.meta a:hover{color:var(--text-primary);text-decoration:underline}
.category-pill{display:inline-block;padding:4px 12px;border-radius:999px;background:var(--brand-orange);color:#fff!important;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;text-decoration:none!important;border:1px solid color-mix(in oklab,#000 10%,var(--brand-orange))}.category-pill:hover{background:color-mix(in oklab,var(--brand-orange) 90%,#000)}.title{font-size:clamp(32px,5vw,48px);line-height:1.2;margin-bottom:24px}.tags{display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;justify-content:center;gap:8px}.tag{display:inline-block;padding:4px 12px;border-radius:999px;background:var(--surface-2);border:1px solid var(--ring);color:var(--text-secondary);font-size:13px;text-decoration:none;font-weight:600}.tag:hover{background:var(--surface);color:var(--text-primary)}

// ===== src/components/CommentsSection.astro =====
// --- UPDATED: Now supports internationalization (i18n) ---
import { getCommentsForReview, type Comment } from '../services/api';
import type { Locale } from '../i18n';
import { useTranslations } from '../lib/i18n';

interface Props {
  reviewId: string;
  lang?: Locale;
}
const { reviewId, lang = 'en' } = Astro.props;
const t = useTranslations(lang);

const comments = await getCommentsForReview(reviewId);

const totalComments = comments.length;
const averageRating = totalComments > 0
  ? (comments.reduce((sum, comment) => sum + comment.rating, 0) / totalComments)
  : 0;

const stars = (rating: number) => {
  const full = Math.max(0, Math.min(5, Math.round(rating)));
  return '★★★★★☆☆☆☆☆'.slice(5 - full, 10 - full);
};

const formatDate = (dateString: string) => {
    return new Date(dateString).toLocaleDateString(lang === 'hi' ? 'hi-IN' : 'en-IN', {
        day: 'numeric',
        month: 'long',
        year: 'numeric'
    });
};
---
{totalComments > 0 && (
  <section class="comments-section" aria-labelledby="comments-title">
    <div class="comments-header">
      <h2 id="comments-title">{t('reviewPost.playerReviews')} ({totalComments})</h2>
      <div class="average-rating">
        <span class="avg-score">{averageRating.toFixed(1)}</span>
        <span class="avg-stars" aria-label={`${t('reviewPost.averageRating')}: ${averageRating.toFixed(1)} / 5`}>
          {stars(averageRating)}
        </span>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="comments-list">
      {comments.map((comment: Comment) => (
        <article class="comment-card">
          <header class="comment-card-header">
            <div class="author-info">
              <div class="avatar">{comment.username.charAt(0)}</div>
              <span class="username">{comment.username}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="rating-info">
              <span class="comment-stars" aria-label={`${t('reviewPost.rated')} ${comment.rating} / 5`}>{stars(comment.rating)}</span>
              <time datetime={comment.createdAt} class="comment-date">{formatDate(comment.createdAt)}</time>
            </div>
          </header>
          <p class="comment-text">{comment.text}</p>
        </article>
      ))}
    </div>
  </section>
)}

<style>
/* Styles remain unchanged */
.comments-section { margin-top: 48px; background-color: var(--surface-2); border: 1px solid var(--ring); border-radius: 16px; padding: clamp(20px, 4vw, 32px); }
.comments-header { display: flex; flex-wrap: wrap; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; gap: 16px; padding-bottom: 16px; border-bottom: 1px solid var(--ring); margin-bottom: 24px; }
#comments-title { font-size: clamp(20px, 3vw, 24px); margin: 0; }
.average-rating { display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 8px; background-color: var(--surface); padding: 8px 12px; border-radius: 12px; border: 1px solid var(--ring); }
.avg-score { font-size: 18px; font-weight: 700; color: var(--text-primary); }
.avg-stars { font-family: ui-sans-serif, system-ui, -apple-system, Segoe UI, Roboto, 'Helvetica Neue', Arial; letter-spacing: 1px; color: var(--brand-gold); }
.comments-list { display: grid; gap: 20px; }
.comment-card { background-color: var(--surface); border: 1px solid var(--ring); border-radius: 12px; padding: 16px; }

// ===== src/components/CrossLinkStrip.astro =====

---
/**
 * CrossLinkStrip.astro
 * --- REFACTORED: Now uses the centralized 'useTranslations' utility. ---
 */

import { getPromotions, getReviews, type Promotion, type ReviewListItem } from '../services/api';
import type { Locale } from '../i18n';
import { useTranslations } from '../lib/i18n'; // <-- IMPORT the new utility

interface Props {
  showPromotions?: boolean;
  showReviews?: boolean;
  titlePromos?: string;
  titleReviews?: string;
  limitPromos?: number;
  limitReviews?: number;
  matchTerms?: string[];
  excludeSlug?: string;
  lang?: Locale;
}

const {
  showPromotions = false,
  showReviews = false,
  titlePromos = 'Current Promotions — Starsuu7 (UU7 • 777)',
  titleReviews = 'Popular Reviews — Starsuu7 (UU7 • 777)',
  limitPromos = 6,
  limitReviews = 6,
  matchTerms = [],
  excludeSlug,
  lang = 'en'
} = Astro.props as Props;

// --- UPDATED: Get the translation function for the current language ---
const t = useTranslations(lang);

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const abs = (p?: string) => (!p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : `${API_BASE_URL}${p}`));

const needles = matchTerms
  .map((t) => String(t || '').toLowerCase().trim())
  .filter(Boolean);

const promosAll = showPromotions && getPromotions ? await getPromotions(lang).catch(() => []) : [];
const reviewsAll = showReviews && getReviews ? await getReviews(lang).catch(() => []) : [];

const scoreText = (text: string): number => {
  if (!needles.length || !text) return 0;
  const hay = text.toLowerCase();
  let s = 0;
  for (const n of needles) if (n && hay.includes(n)) s += 1;
  return s;
};

const scoredPromos = promosAll
  .filter((p) => p.imageUrl && (!excludeSlug || p.slug !== excludeSlug))
  .map((p) => ({
    ...p,
    _score:
      scoreText(`${p.title} ${p.subtitle ?? ''} ${p.description ?? ''}`) +
      scoreText((p.details || []).join(' ')),
  }))
  .sort((a, b) => {
    if (b._score !== a._score) return b._score - a._score;
    return 0;
  })
  .slice(0, limitPromos);

const scoredReviews = reviewsAll
  .filter((r) => r.image && (!excludeSlug || r.slug !== excludeSlug))
  .map((r) => ({
    ...r,
    _score: scoreText(`${r.title} ${r.excerpt ?? ''} ${r.gameName ?? ''}`),
  }))
  .sort((a, b) => {
    if (b._score !== a._score) return b._score - a._score;
    const ar = Number.isFinite(+a.rating) ? +a.rating : -1;
    const br = Number.isFinite(+b.rating) ? +b.rating : -1;
    if (br !== ar) return br - ar;
    return 0;
  })
  .slice(0, limitReviews);

const hasPromos = showPromotions && scoredPromos.length > 0;
const hasReviews = showReviews && scoredReviews.length > 0;
const renderAnything = hasPromos || hasReviews;
---

{renderAnything && (
  <section class="xlinks" aria-label="Internal linking">
    <div class="container">
      {hasPromos && (
        <div class="strip">
          <header class="head">
            <h2>{titlePromos}</h2>
            {/* UPDATED: Use the 't' function with a key from our JSON file */}
            <p class="muted" set:html={t('crossLinkStrip.descPromos')}></p>
          </header>

          <div class="grid promos">
            {scoredPromos.map((p: Promotion) => {
              const href = `/promotions/${p.slug}`;
              const img = abs(p.imageUrl);
              const badge = p.badgeText || '';
              return (
                <article class="card promo">
                  <a href={href} class="artlink" aria-label={`View promotion: ${p.title}`}>
                    {img && <img src={img} alt="" width="480" height="300" loading="lazy" class="cover" />}
                    {badge && <span class="badge">{badge}</span>}
                  </a>
                  <div class="content">
                    <h3 class="title"><a href={href}>{p.title}</a></h3>
                    {p.subtitle && <p class="subtitle">{p.subtitle}</p>}
                    {p.description && <p class="excerpt">{p.description}</p>}
                    <a class="cta" href={href}>Learn more</a>
                  </div>
                </article>
              );
            })}
          </div>

          <div class="more">
            {/* UPDATED: Use the 't' function */}
            <a class="btn ghost" href="/promotions/" aria-label={t('crossLinkStrip.seeAllPromos')}>
              {t('crossLinkStrip.seeAllPromos')}
            </a>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {hasReviews && (
        <div class="strip">
          <header class="head">
            <h2>{titleReviews}</h2>
            {/* UPDATED: Use the 't' function */}
            <p class="muted" set:html={t('crossLinkStrip.descReviews')}></p>
          </header>

          <div class="grid reviews">
            {scoredReviews.map((r: ReviewListItem) => {
              const href = `/reviews/${r.slug}`;
              const img = abs(r.image);
              const stars = Number.isFinite(+r.rating) ? Math.max(0, Math.min(5, Math.round(+r.rating))) : 0;
              return (
                <article class="card review">
                  <a href={href} class="artlink" aria-label={`Read review: ${r.title}`}>
                    {img && <img src={img} alt="" width="480" height="300" loading="lazy" class="cover" />}
                    {stars > 0 && <span class="rating" aria-label={`${stars} out of 5`}>{'★'.repeat(stars)}{'☆'.repeat(5 - stars)}</span>}
                  </a>
                  <div class="content">
                    <h3 class="title"><a href={href}>{r.title}</a></h3>
                    {r.gameName && <p class="meta"><strong>Game:</strong> {r.gameName}</p>}
                    {r.excerpt && <p class="excerpt">{r.excerpt}</p>}
                    <a class="cta" href={href}>Read full review</a>
                  </div>
                </article>
              );
            })}
          </div>

          <div class="more">
            {/* UPDATED: Use the 't' function */}
            <a class="btn ghost" href="/reviews/" aria-label={t('crossLinkStrip.seeAllReviews')}>
              {t('crossLinkStrip.seeAllReviews')}
            </a>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  </section>
)}

  version?: string;
  size?: string;
  updated?: string;
  theme?: 'gold' | 'emerald' | 'violet' | 'azure';
  lang?: Locale;
}

const scriptTranslations = t('downloadCta.script');

const settings = await getSettings();
let releaseData: Record<string, string> = {};
try {
  releaseData = (await import('../data/release.json')).default;
} catch (_) {}

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const downloadUrl = settings?.apkDownloadLink || releaseData.downloadUrl || '#';
const qrCodeUrl = settings?.qrCodeImageUrl ? `${API_BASE_URL}${settings.qrCodeImageUrl}` : null;

const version = props.version ?? releaseData.version ?? '—';
const size = props.size ?? releaseData.size ?? '—';
const updated = props.updated ?? releaseData.updated ?? '—';

<script is:inline>
  // --- SCRIPT UPDATED to read from data attributes ---
  function haptic(){ try { navigator.vibrate && navigator.vibrate(12); } catch(_) {} }
  function track(name, params){
    try { if (window.gtag) window.gtag('event', name, params || {}); } catch(_){}
  }
  function isAndroid(){ return /Android/i.test(navigator.userAgent || ''); }

  document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
    const t = e.target;
    if (!(t instanceof Element)) return;
    const copyBtn = t.closest('[data-copy]');
    if (!(copyBtn instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
    
    e.preventDefault();
    const text = copyBtn.dataset.clipboard || '';
    const originalText = copyBtn.dataset.copyText || 'Copy Link';
    const copiedText = copyBtn.dataset.copiedText || 'Copied!';
    const errorText = copyBtn.dataset.copyErrorText || 'Press Ctrl/Cmd+C';
    
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(() => {
      copyBtn.textContent = copiedText;
      copyBtn.classList.add('copied');
      haptic();
      track('download_copy', { method: 'copy_button' });
      setTimeout(() => { copyBtn.textContent = originalText; copyBtn.classList.remove('copied'); }, 1500);
    }).catch(() => {
      copyBtn.textContent = errorText;
      setTimeout(() => { copyBtn.textContent = originalText; }, 1500);
    });
  }, { passive: false });
  
  function onDownloadTap(e){
    const el = e.currentTarget;
    if (!(el instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
    const label = el.getAttribute('data-analytics') || 'download_unknown';
    const version = el.getAttribute('data-version') || '';
    const size = el.getAttribute('data-size') || '';
    track(label, { location: label, version, size });
    haptic();
    maybeShowInstallHelper();
  }
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-analytics="download_apk"], [data-analytics="download_fab"], [data-analytics="download_mirror"]').forEach((a) => {
    a.addEventListener('click', onDownloadTap, { passive: true });
  });
  
  (function(){
    const fab = document.querySelector('[data-dl-fab]');
    if (!(fab instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
    if (!('IntersectionObserver' in window)) return;
    const targets = ['.site-footer', '#download'].map((s)=>document.querySelector(s)).filter((el) => el instanceof Element);
    if (!targets.length) return;
    const obs = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
      const visible = entries.some((e)=>e.isIntersecting);
      fab.style.opacity = visible ? '0' : '1';
      fab.style.pointerEvents = visible ? 'none' : 'auto';
      fab.style.transform = visible ? 'translateY(8px)' : 'translateY(0)';
    }, { rootMargin: '0px 0px -25% 0px', threshold: 0.01 });
    targets.forEach((t)=>t && obs.observe(t));
  })();
  
  function maybeShowInstallHelper(){
    if (!isAndroid()) return;
    if (sessionStorage.getItem('apk_install_helper_shown')) return;
    const toast = document.querySelector('.install-toast');
    if (!(toast instanceof HTMLElement)) return;

    // --- NEW: Populate toast from data attributes ---
    const { toastTitle, toastStep1, toastStep2, toastStep3, toastDismiss } = toast.dataset;
    const titleEl = toast.querySelector('strong');
    const stepsEl = toast.querySelectorAll('ol li');
    const dismissBtn = toast.querySelector('.toast-dismiss');
    if(titleEl) titleEl.innerHTML = toastTitle || '';
    if(stepsEl[0]) stepsEl[0].innerHTML = toastStep1 || '';
    if(stepsEl[1]) stepsEl[1].innerHTML = toastStep2 || '';
    if(stepsEl[2]) stepsEl[2].innerHTML = toastStep3 || '';
    if(dismissBtn) dismissBtn.textContent = toastDismiss || 'Got it';
    // --- END NEW ---

    toast.hidden = false;
    toast.classList.add('show');
    sessionStorage.setItem('apk_install_helper_shown', '1');
    const hide = () => { toast.classList.remove('show'); setTimeout(()=>toast.hidden = true, 180); };
    const timer = setTimeout(hide, 10000);
    if (dismissBtn) dismissBtn.addEventListener('click', () => { clearTimeout(timer); hide(); }, { passive: true });
  }
</script>

// ===== src/components/FAQ.astro =====
// --- REFACTORED: Now uses the centralized 'useTranslations' utility ---
// --- FIXED: Added type-safe handling for the FAQ list ---

import type { Locale } from '../i18n';
import { useTranslations } from '../lib/i18n';

interface Props {
  lang?: Locale;
}
const { lang = 'en' } = Astro.props as Props;

const t = useTranslations(lang);

const title = t('faq.title');
const description = t('faq.description');
const viewAllText = t('faq.viewAll');

// --- THE FIX: Check if the returned value is an array before assigning it ---
const faqListResult = t('faq.list');

<section id="faq" class="faq-section">
  <div class="container">
    <header class="section-head">

          </summary>
          <div class="answer">

          </div>
        </details>
      ))}
    </div>

    <div class="more-link-container">
      <a href="/faq/" class="btn-view-all">
        {viewAllText}
      </a>
    </div>

  </div>
</section>

// --- REFACTOR: All links are now language-aware using the createPath utility ---

import BadgeIcon from './BadgeIcon.astro';
import { getSettings } from '../services/api';
import type { Locale } from '../i18n';
import { useTranslations } from '../lib/i18n';
import { createPath } from '../lib/paths'; // <-- IMPORT the new utility

interface Props {
  lang?: Locale;
}
const { lang = 'en' } = Astro.props as Props;
const t = useTranslations(lang);

const settings = await getSettings();
const year = new Date().getFullYear();

// --- UPDATED: home link is now language-aware ---
const brandInfo = {
  name: settings?.siteName || "Starsuu7",
  tagline: t('footer.tagline'),
  homeUrl: createPath('/', lang)
};

const potentialSocials = [
  { key: 'youtubeUrl', imgSrc: "/wordpress/youtube.png", label: 'YouTube' },
  { key: 'facebookUrl', imgSrc: "/wordpress/facebook.png", label: 'Facebook' },
  { key: 'instagramUrl', imgSrc: "/wordpress/instagram.webp", label: 'Instagram' },
  { key: 'telegramUrl', imgSrc: "/wordpress/telegram.png", label: 'Telegram' },
  { key: 'whatsappUrl', imgSrc: "/wordpress/whatsapp.png", label: 'WhatsApp' },
  { key: 'twitterUrl', imgSrc: "/wordpress/x.webp", label: 'Twitter' },
];

const socialLinks = settings
  ? potentialSocials
      .map(s => ({ ...s, href: settings[s.key as keyof typeof settings] as string }))
      .filter(s => s.href)
  : [];

// --- UPDATED: All hrefs are now built dynamically using createPath ---
const navLinks = [
  { href: createPath("/", lang), label: t('footer.nav.home') },
  { href: createPath("/#games", lang), label: t('footer.nav.games') },
  { href: createPath("/faq/", lang), label: t('footer.nav.faq') },
  { href: createPath("/#about", lang), label: t('footer.nav.about') }
];

const legalLinks = [
  { href: createPath("/privacy-policy/", lang), label: t('footer.legalNav.privacy') },
  { href: createPath("/terms-of-service/", lang), label: t('footer.legalNav.terms') },
  { href: createPath("/responsible-gaming/", lang), label: t('footer.legalNav.responsible') }
];
// --- END UPDATE ---

const integrityBadges = [
  { icon: 'no-bot', text: t('footer.integrityBadges.noBot') },
  { icon: 'iso', text: t('footer.integrityBadges.iso') },
  { icon: 'withdrawal', text: t('footer.integrityBadges.withdrawal') },
  { icon: 'rng', text: t('footer.integrityBadges.rng') },
];

const paymentPartners = [
  { imgSrc: "/wordpress/payment-1.webp", alt: "Paytm" },
  { imgSrc: "/wordpress/payment5-2.webp", alt: "RuPay" },
  { imgSrc: "/wordpress/payment7.webp", alt: "PhonePe" },
  { imgSrc: "/wordpress/payment6-2.webp", alt: "UPI" },
  { imgSrc: "/wordpress/payment2-2.webp", alt: "Visa" },
  { imgSrc: "/wordpress/payment4-2.webp", alt: "Mastercard" },
];

// ===== src/components/GameGrid.astro =====

// ===== src/components/GameGrid.astro =====
// --- REFACTORED: Now uses the centralized 'useTranslations' utility. ---

import { getReviews } from '../services/api';
import type { ReviewListItem } from '../services/api';
import type { Locale } from '../i18n';
import { useTranslations } from '../lib/i18n'; // <-- IMPORT the new utility

interface Props {
  lang?: Locale;
}
const { lang = 'en' } = Astro.props as Props;

// --- UPDATED: Get the translation function for the current language ---
const t = useTranslations(lang);

const allReviews = await getReviews(lang);
const reviews = allReviews.filter(r => r.image).slice(0, 8);

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;

function stars(rating: number): string {
  const num = Number.isFinite(rating) ? rating : 0;
  const full = Math.max(0, Math.min(5, Math.round(num)));
  return '★★★★★☆☆☆☆☆'.slice(5 - full, 10 - full);
}
---
<section id="games" class="game-grid-section">
  <div class="container">
    <header class="section-head">
      {/* UPDATED: Use the 't' function with a key from our JSON file */}
      <h2>{t('gameGrid.title')}</h2>
      <p class="muted">{t('gameGrid.description')}</p>
    </header>
    <div class="grid">
      {reviews.map((review: ReviewListItem) => {
        const imageUrl = review.image.startsWith('http') ? review.image : `${API_BASE_URL}${review.image}`;
        const reviewUrl = `/reviews/${review.slug}`;
        
        return (
          <a href={reviewUrl} class="game-card">
            <img src={imageUrl} alt={review.title} class="art" loading="lazy" width="300" height="400" />
            <div class="overlay">
              {/* Note: aria-label for stars is not easily translatable with this setup, keeping it simple */}
              <div class="rating" aria-label={`Rating: ${review.rating} out of 5 stars`}>
                {stars(review.rating)}
              </div>
              <div class="content">
                <h3 class="title">{review.title}</h3>
                <span class="category">{review.gameName}</span>
                {/* UPDATED: Use the 't' function */}
                <span class="cta">{t('gameGrid.cta')}</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </a>
        );
      })}
    </div>

    <div class="more-link-container">
      {/* UPDATED: Use the 't' function */}
      <a href="/reviews/" class="btn-view-all">
        {t('gameGrid.seeAll')}
      </a>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<script is:inline>
  // Script remains unchanged
  (function(){ const menu = document.querySelector('details[data-mobile-menu]'); const summary = menu?.querySelector('summary.hamburger'); const sheet = menu?.querySelector('.sheet'); if (!menu || !summary || !sheet) return; function openMenu() { menu.setAttribute('open', ''); } function closeMenu() { menu.removeAttribute('open'); } summary.addEventListener('click', (e) => { e.preventDefault(); menu.hasAttribute('open') ? closeMenu() : openMenu(); }, { passive: false }); summary.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') { e.preventDefault(); menu.hasAttribute('open') ? closeMenu() : openMenu(); } }); document.addEventListener('click', (e) => { if (!menu.hasAttribute('open')) return; const t = e.target; if (!(t instanceof Element)) return; if (!t.closest('details[data-mobile-menu]')) closeMenu(); }); sheet.addEventListener('click', (e) => { const t = e.target; if (t instanceof Element && t.closest('a')) closeMenu(); }); function haptic(){ try { navigator.vibrate && navigator.vibrate(12); } catch(_) {} } document.addEventListener('click', (e) => { const el = e.target; const a = el && el.closest && el.closest('[data-analytics]'); if (!a) return; const name = a.getAttribute('data-analytics') || 'nav_click'; try { if (window.gtag) window.gtag('event', name, { label: name }); } catch(_){} haptic(); }, { passive: true }); })();
</script>

// src/components/HowToPlay.astro
// --- REFACTORED: Now uses the centralized 'useTranslations' utility ---
// --- FIXED: Correctly injects JSON-LD to prevent parsing errors ---

import type { Locale } from '../i18n';
import { useTranslations } from '../lib/i18n';

interface Props {
  lang?: Locale;
}
const { lang = 'en' } = Astro.props as Props;
const t = useTranslations(lang);

// --- UPDATED: Fetch all content dynamically from the locale file ---
const title = t('howToPlay.title');
const description = t('howToPlay.description');
const viewAllText = t('howToPlay.viewAll');

// Type-safe check for the steps array
const stepsResult = t('howToPlay.steps');
const steps: { title: string; body: string }[] = Array.isArray(stepsResult) ? stepsResult : [];

// Build HowTo JSON-LD from the translated steps
const howToJsonLd = {
  "@context": "https://schema.org",
  "@type": "HowTo",
  "name": title, // Use translated title
  "description": description, // Use translated description
  "step": steps.map((s, idx) => ({
    "@type": "HowToStep",
    "position": idx + 1,
    "name": s.title,
    "url": `#how-step-${idx + 1}`,
    "itemListElement": [
      {
        "@type": "HowToDirection",
        "text": s.body
      }
    ]
  }))
};
---

<section id="how" class="how-to-play-section" aria-labelledby="howto-title">
  <div class="container">
    <header class="section-head">
      {/* UPDATED: Dynamic text */}
      <h2 id="howto-title">{title}</h2>
      <p class="muted">{description}</p>
    </header>

    {/* --- THE FIX --- 
        Use the `set:html` directive to correctly inject the stringified JSON.
    */}
    <script type="application/ld+json" set:html={JSON.stringify(howToJsonLd)}></script>

    <div class="grid">
      {/* UPDATED: Map over dynamic steps and add 'num' property */}
      {steps.map((step, index) => (
        <div class="step-card" id={`how-step-${index + 1}`}>
          <div class="number" aria-hidden="true">{index + 1}</div>
          <h3 class="title">{step.title}</h3>
          <p class="body">{step.body}</p>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>

    <div class="more-link-container">
      {/* UPDATED: Dynamic button text */}
      <a href="/blog/" class="btn-view-all">
        {viewAllText}
      </a>
    </div>

  </div>
</section>

// ===== src/components/LanguageSwitcher.astro =====

---
import { useI18n, locales } from "../i18n";

const { getLocalePath, locale: currentLocale } = useI18n(Astro);

const languageNames: Record<string, string> = {
  en: 'English',
  hi: 'हिंदी',
};

const currentLanguageName = languageNames[currentLocale] || currentLocale.toUpperCase();
---
<div class="language-switcher" role="region" aria-label="Language selection">
  <button class="switcher-toggle" type="button" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="language-drawer">
    <span>{currentLanguageName}</span>
  </button>

  <div class="switcher-drawer" id="language-drawer" role="menu" aria-hidden="true">
    <div class="drawer-inner">
      {locales.map((locale) => {
        if (locale === currentLocale) {
          return (
            <span class="switcher-item is-active" aria-current="page" role="menuitem">
              {languageNames[locale] || locale.toUpperCase()}
            </span>
          );
        }
        return (
          <a href={getLocalePath(locale)} class="switcher-item" hreflang={locale} data-astro-reload role="menuitem">
            {languageNames[locale] || locale.toUpperCase()}
          </a>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<style>
  .language-switcher {
    position: fixed;
    top: 50%;
    right: 0;
    transform: translateY(-50%);
    z-index: 1000;
    display: flex;
    flex-direction: row-reverse;
    align-items: stretch;
  }

  /* The clickable tab */
  .switcher-toggle {
    appearance: none;
    /* --- UPDATED: Use brand color for fill --- */
    background-color: var(--brand-orange);
    /* --- UPDATED: Use white for border --- */
    border: 1px solid #ffffff;
    border-right: none;
    border-top-left-radius: 12px;
    border-bottom-left-radius: 12px;
    padding: 16px 8px;
    cursor: pointer;
    box-shadow: var(--shadow-lg);
    z-index: 2;
  }
  .switcher-toggle span {
    writing-mode: vertical-rl;
    font-weight: 700;
    /* --- UPDATED: Use white for text for better contrast --- */
    color: #ffffff;
    font-size: 14px;
    text-orientation: mixed;
  }

  /* The drawer containing language links */
  .switcher-drawer {
    background-color: var(--surface);
    border: 1px solid var(--ring);
    border-right: 1px solid var(--ring);
    border-top-left-radius: 12px;
    border-bottom-left-radius: 12px;
    box-shadow: var(--shadow-lg);
    overflow: hidden;
    z-index: 1;
    transition: max-width 0.4s cubic-bezier(0.22, 1, 0.36, 1), opacity 0.3s ease-out;
    max-width: 0;
    opacity: 0;
  }
  .drawer-inner {
    white-space: nowrap;
  }

  /* Expanded State */
  .language-switcher.is-open .switcher-drawer {
    max-width: 200px;
    opacity: 1;
  }

  .switcher-item {
    display: block;
    padding: 12px 24px;
    font-size: 14px;
    font-weight: 600;
    text-decoration: none;
    color: var(--text-secondary);
    transition: background-color 0.2s, color 0.2s;
  }
  .switcher-item:not(:last-child) { 
    border-bottom: 1px solid var(--ring); 
  }
  .switcher-item:hover { 
    background-color: var(--surface-2); 
    color: var(--text-primary); 
  }
  .switcher-item.is-active {
    background-color: var(--brand-orange);
    color: white;
    font-weight: 700;
    cursor: default;
  }
</style>

<script>
  const switcher = document.querySelector('.language-switcher');
  const toggleBtn = document.querySelector('.switcher-toggle');
  const drawer = document.getElementById('language-drawer');
  
  if (switcher && toggleBtn && drawer) {
    const closeDrawer = () => {
      switcher.classList.remove('is-open');
      toggleBtn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
      drawer.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
    };
    
    toggleBtn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.stopPropagation();
      const isOpen = switcher.classList.toggle('is-open');
      toggleBtn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', String(isOpen));
      drawer.setAttribute('aria-hidden', String(!isOpen));
    });

    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      if (switcher.classList.contains('is-open') && !switcher.contains(e.target as Node)) {
        closeDrawer();
      }
    });

    document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
      if (e.key === 'Escape' && switcher.classList.contains('is-open')) {
        closeDrawer();
      }
    });
  }
</script>

// ===== src/components/MobileAppShell.astro =====

---
// ===== src/components/MobileAppShell.astro =====
// --- REFACTORED: All links now use the createPath utility for language-awareness ---
import type { Locale } from '../i18n';
import { useTranslations } from '../lib/i18n';
import { createPath } from '../lib/paths'; // <-- IMPORT the new utility

interface Props {
  title?: string;
  active?: 'home' | 'blog' | 'promos' | 'download' | 'faq';
  showBack?: boolean;
  promoBadge?: number;
  showFab?: boolean;
  lang?: Locale;
}
const {
  title = 'Starsuu7',
  active = 'home',
  showBack = false,
  promoBadge = 0,
  showFab = true,
  lang = 'en'
} = Astro.props as Props;

const t = useTranslations(lang);

// --- UPDATED: All hrefs are now built dynamically using createPath ---
const homePath = createPath('/', lang);
const blogPath = createPath('/blog/', lang);

<script is:inline>
  // Script remains unchanged
  document.addEventListener('click', (e) => { const el = e.target; if (!(el instanceof Element)) return; const btn = el.closest('[data-action]'); if (!btn) return; const action = btn.getAttribute('data-action'); if (action === 'back') { e.preventDefault(); if (history.length > 1) history.back(); } if (action === 'menu') { e.preventDefault(); if (window.AppMenu && typeof window.AppMenu.open === 'function') { window.AppMenu.open(); } else { window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('open-global-menu')); } } }, { passive: false }); function haptic(){ try{ navigator.vibrate && navigator.vibrate(12); } catch{} } document.querySelectorAll('.tabbar a').forEach(a => a.addEventListener('click', () => haptic(), { passive: true })); function isSamePageHashLink(a){ if (!a.hash) return false; const currentPath = window.location.pathname.replace(/\/hi\//, '/'); return a.pathname === currentPath || a.pathname.replace(/\/$/, '') === currentPath.replace(/\/$/, ''); } function offsetTopFor(id){ const el = document.querySelector(id); if(!el) return 0; const bar = document.querySelector('.app-bar'); const h = bar ? bar.getBoundingClientRect().height : 60; const y = el.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.scrollY; return Math.max(0, y - h - 8); } function smoothTo(hash){ const y = offsetTopFor(hash); window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' }); } document.querySelectorAll('.tabbar a').forEach((a) => { a.addEventListener('click', (e) => { if (!isSamePageHashLink(a)) return; e.preventDefault(); haptic(); smoothTo(a.hash); history.pushState(null,'',a.hash); }, { passive: false }); }); const fab = document.querySelector('[data-fab]'); if (fab && 'IntersectionObserver' in window) { const targets = ['.site-footer'].map(s => document.querySelector(s)).filter(Boolean); if (targets.length) { const obs = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => { const visible = entries.some(e => e.isIntersecting); fab.style.opacity = visible ? '0' : '1'; fab.style.pointerEvents = visible ? 'none' : 'auto'; fab.style.transform = visible ? 'translateY(8px)' : 'translateY(0)'; }, { rootMargin: '0px 0px -20% 0px', threshold: 0.01 }); targets.forEach(t => obs.observe(t)); } }
</script>

import type { Locale } from '../i18n';
import { useTranslations } from '../lib/i18n';

interface Props {
  lang?: Locale;
}
const { lang = 'en' } = Astro.props as Props;
const t = useTranslations(lang);

// This banner image is not language-dependent, so it remains static.
const promoBanners = [
  "/wordpress/promotion-768x1095.webp",
];

// --- UPDATED: Fetch all content dynamically from the locale file ---
const promoTitle = t('promoHowToPlay.promoTitle');
const howToTitle = t('promoHowToPlay.howToTitle');
const seeAllText = t('promoHowToPlay.seeAll');

// Type-safe check for the steps array
const stepsResult = t('promoHowToPlay.steps');
const howToPlayContent: { title: string; text?: string; list?: string[] }[] = Array.isArray(stepsResult) ? stepsResult : [];
---
<section id="promos" class="promo-how-section">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="promo-box">
      <div class="grid">
        <!-- Left Column: Promotions -->
        <div class="column">
          {/* UPDATED: Dynamic title */}
          <h2 class="section-title">{promoTitle}</h2>
          <div class="promo-banners">
            {promoBanners.map(src => (
              <img src={src} alt="Promotion banner" loading="lazy" width="768" height="1095" />
            ))}
          </div>
          
          <div class="more-promos-link">
            {/* UPDATED: Dynamic button text */}
            <a href="/promotions/" class="btn-view-all-promos" set:html={seeAllText}></a>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <!-- Right Column: How To Play -->
        <div class="column">
          {/* UPDATED: Dynamic title */}
          <h2 class="section-title">{howToTitle}</h2>
          <div class="how-to-cards">
            {/* UPDATED: Map over dynamic steps */}
            {howToPlayContent.map(item => (
              <div class="how-to-card">
                <h3>{item.title}</h3>
                {item.text && <p>{item.text}</p>}
                {item.list && (
                  <ol>
                    {item.list.map(li => <li>{li}</li>)}
                  </ol>
                )}
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

import type { Locale } from '../i18n';
import { useTranslations } from '../lib/i18n';

interface Props {
  lang?: Locale;
}
const { lang = 'en' } = Astro.props as Props;

// --- UPDATED: Fetch all content dynamically from the locale file ---
const title = t('promotions.title');
const description = t('promotions.description');
const viewAllText = t('promotions.viewAll');

// Type-safe check for the steps array
const stepsResult = t('promotions.steps');
const promoSteps: { num: number; title: string; body: string }[] = Array.isArray(stepsResult) 
  ? stepsResult.map((step, index) => ({ ...step, num: index + 1 })) 
  : [];
---
<section class="promos-section-steps">
  <div class="container">
    <header class="section-head">
      {/* UPDATED: Use dynamic text */}
      <h2>{title}</h2>
      <p class="muted">{description}</p>
    </header>

    <div class="grid">
      {/* UPDATED: Map over dynamic steps */}
      {promoSteps.map(step => (
        <div class="step-card">
          <div class="number" aria-hidden="true">{step.num}</div>
          <h3 class="title">{step.title}</h3>
          <p class="body">{step.body}</p>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
    
    <div class="more-link-container">
      {/* UPDATED: Use dynamic button text */}
      <a href="/promotions/" class="btn-view-all">
        {viewAllText}
      </a>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

// ===== src/components/RecentBlogs.astro =====
// --- REFACTORED: Now uses the centralized 'useTranslations' utility ---

import { getBlogPosts } from '../services/api';
import type { BlogPostListItem } from '../services/api';
import type { Locale } from '../i18n';
import { useTranslations } from '../lib/i18n';

interface Props {
  lang?: Locale;
}
const { lang = 'en' } = Astro.props as Props;
const t = useTranslations(lang);

// --- UPDATED: Fetch localized blog posts based on the 'lang' prop ---
const allPosts = await getBlogPosts(lang);
const recentPosts = allPosts.filter(post => post.image).slice(0, 3);

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
---
{/* Only render the section if there are posts to display */}
{recentPosts.length > 0 && (
  <section class="recent-blogs-section">
    <div class="container">
      <header class="section-head">
        <div>
          {/* UPDATED: Dynamic text */}
          <h2>{t('recentBlogs.title')}</h2>
          <p class="muted">{t('recentBlogs.description')}</p>
        </div>
        {/* UPDATED: Dynamic text */}
        <a href="/blog/" class="btn-view-all">{t('recentBlogs.viewAll')}</a>
      </header>

      <div class="post-grid">
        {recentPosts.map((post: BlogPostListItem) => {
          const postUrl = `/blog/${post.slug}`;
          const imageUrl = post.image.startsWith('http') ? post.image : `${API_BASE_URL}${post.image}`;
          const formattedDate = new Date(post.publishedAt).toLocaleDateString('en-IN', {
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'
          });

          return (
            <article class="post-card">
              <a href={postUrl} class="card-image-link" aria-label={`Read more about ${post.title}`}>
                <img src={imageUrl} alt="" loading="lazy" width="400" height="250" class="card-image" />
              </a>
              <div class="card-content">
                <p class="card-meta">
                  <time datetime={post.publishedAt}>{formattedDate}</time>
                </p>
                <h3 class="card-title">
                  <a href={postUrl}>{post.title}</a>
                </h3>
                <p class="card-excerpt">{post.excerpt}</p>
                {/* UPDATED: Dynamic text */}
                <a href={postUrl} class="read-more-link" aria-label={`Read more about ${post.title}`}>{t('recentBlogs.readMore')}</a>
              </div>
            </article>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  </section>
)}

// ===== src/components/RelatedPromotions.astro =====

---
/**
 * RelatedPromotions.astro
 * Internal-linking block to surface relevant promos and strengthen topical clusters
 * for Starsuu7 / UU7 / 777 across the site.
 *
 * Props:
 *  - title?: string                 // default: "Related Promotions — Starsuu7 (UU7 • 777)"
 *  - limit?: number                 // default: 6
 *  - matchTerms?: string[]          // optional: keywords to match against title/subtitle/description
 *  - excludeSlug?: string           // optional: avoid self-linking on detail pages
 *  - showCTA?: boolean              // default: true (adds “See all promotions” link)
 *
 * Usage (promotion detail page):
 *   <RelatedPromotions matchTerms={[promo.title, ...promo.details]} excludeSlug={promo.slug} />
 *
 * Usage (blog/review pages):
 *   <RelatedPromotions matchTerms={['teen patti','rummy','bonus']} limit={3} />
 */

let getPromotions: undefined | ((lang?: string) => Promise<any[]>);
try {
  const mod = await import('../services/api');
  // @ts-ignore tolerate missing export during SSR
  getPromotions = mod.getPromotions;
} catch {}

interface Props {
  title?: string;
  limit?: number;
  matchTerms?: string[];
  excludeSlug?: string;
  showCTA?: boolean;
}

const {
  title = 'Related Promotions — Starsuu7 (UU7 • 777)',
  limit = 6,
  matchTerms = [],
  excludeSlug,
  showCTA = true
} = Astro.props as Props;

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const toAbs = (p?: string) =>
  !p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : `${API_BASE_URL}${p}`);

const all = getPromotions ? await getPromotions('en').catch(() => [] as any[]) : ([] as any[]);

// Build a simple matcher over title/subtitle/description/details (strings only)
const needles = matchTerms
  .map((t) => String(t || '').toLowerCase().trim())
  .filter(Boolean);

function scorePromo(p: any): number {
  if (!needles.length) return 0;
  const hay = [
    p?.title, p?.subtitle, p?.description,
    ...(Array.isArray(p?.details) ? p.details : [])
  ]
    .filter(Boolean)
    .map((s: string) => s.toLowerCase())
    .join(' | ');

  let score = 0;
  for (const n of needles) {
    if (!n) continue;
    if (hay.includes(n)) score += 1;
  }
  return score;
}

// Rank by (1) match score (2) displayOrder asc (3) createdAt desc if present
const ranked = all
  .filter((p: any) => !excludeSlug || p.slug !== excludeSlug)
  .map((p: any) => ({ ...p, _score: scorePromo(p) }))
  .sort((a: any, b: any) => {
    if (b._score !== a._score) return b._score - a._score;
    const ao = typeof a.displayOrder === 'number' ? a.displayOrder : Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER;
    const bo = typeof b.displayOrder === 'number' ? b.displayOrder : Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER;
    if (ao !== bo) return ao - bo;
    const ad = new Date(a.createdAt || 0).getTime();
    const bd = new Date(b.createdAt || 0).getTime();
    return bd - ad;
  })
  .slice(0, limit);

const hasData = ranked.length > 0;
---

{hasData && (
  <section class="related-promos" aria-labelledby="related-promos-title">
    <div class="container">
      <header class="section-head">
        <h2 id="related-promos-title">{title}</h2>
        <p class="muted">
          Boost your bankroll with current offers for <strong>Starsuu7</strong> (aka <strong>UU7</strong> • <strong>777</strong>). Terms apply.
        </p>
      </header>

      <div class="grid">
        {ranked.map((p: any) => {
          const href = `/promotions/${p.slug}`;
          const img = toAbs(p.imageUrl);
          const badgeText = p.badgeText || '';
          const badgeColor = p.badgeColor || 'var(--brand-orange)';

          return (
            <article class="promo-card">
              <a href={href} class="image-link" aria-label={`View promotion: ${p.title}`}>
                {img && <img class="cover" src={img} alt="" width="480" height="300" loading="lazy" />}
                {badgeText && <span class="badge" style={`--bcol:${badgeColor}`}>{badgeText}</span>}
              </a>
              <div class="content">
                <h3 class="title">
                  <a href={href}>{p.title}</a>
                </h3>
                {p.subtitle && <p class="subtitle">{p.subtitle}</p>}
                {p.description && <p class="excerpt">{p.description}</p>}
                <a class="cta" href={href} aria-label={`See details: ${p.title}`}>
                  {p.ctaText || 'View details'}
                </a>
              </div>
            </article>
          );
        })}
      </div>

      {showCTA && (
        <div class="more-cta">
          <a class="btn" href="/promotions/" aria-label="See all promotions on Starsuu7">
            See all promotions
          </a>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  </section>
)}

<style>
  .related-promos {
    padding-block: 32px;
    background: var(--surface);
    border-top: 1px solid var(--ring);
  }
  .section-head {
    text-align: center;
    max-width: 720px;
    margin-inline: auto;
    margin-bottom: 24px;
  }
  .section-head h2 {
    font-size: clamp(22px, 3.6vw, 28px);
    margin: 0 0 6px;
  }

  .grid {
    display: grid;
    grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(260px, 1fr));
    gap: 16px;
  }

  .promo-card {

    display: flex;

    transition: transform .2s ease-out, box-shadow .2s ease-out;

  .image-link { display: block; position: relative; }

// ===== src/components/RelatedReviews.astro =====

---
/**
 * RelatedReviews.astro
 * Internal-linking block to surface relevant reviews and strengthen topical clusters
 * for Starsuu7 / UU7 / 777 across the site.
 *
 * Props:
 *  - title?: string                 // default: "Related Reviews — Starsuu7 (UU7 • 777)"
 *  - limit?: number                 // default: 6
 *  - matchTerms?: string[]          // optional: keywords to match against title/excerpt/gameName
 *  - excludeSlug?: string           // optional: avoid self-linking on detail pages
 *  - showCTA?: boolean              // default: true (adds “See all reviews” link)
 *
 * Usage (review detail page):
 *   <RelatedReviews matchTerms={[review.title?.en ?? review.title, review.gameName, ...review.tags]} excludeSlug={review.slug} />
 *
 * Usage (blog/promo pages):
 *   <RelatedReviews matchTerms={['teen patti','rummy','uu7','777']} limit={3} />
 */

let getReviews: undefined | ((lang?: string) => Promise<any[]>);
try {
  const mod = await import('../services/api');
  // @ts-ignore tolerate missing export during SSR
  getReviews = mod.getReviews;
} catch {}

interface Props {
  title?: string;
  limit?: number;
  matchTerms?: string[];
  excludeSlug?: string;
  showCTA?: boolean;
}

const {
  title = 'Related Reviews — Starsuu7 (UU7 • 777)',
  limit = 6,
  matchTerms = [],
  excludeSlug,
  showCTA = true
} = Astro.props as Props;

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const abs = (p?: string) => (!p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : `${API_BASE_URL}${p}`));

const all = getReviews ? await getReviews('en').catch(() => [] as any[]) : ([] as any[]);

// Normalize inputs
const needles = matchTerms
  .map((t) => String(t || '').toLowerCase().trim())
  .filter(Boolean);

// Simple keyword scorer across title/excerpt/gameName
function scoreReview(r: any): number {
  if (!needles.length) return 0;
  const hay = [r?.title, r?.excerpt, r?.gameName]
    .filter(Boolean)
    .map((s: string) => s.toLowerCase())
    .join(' | ');
  let score = 0;
  for (const n of needles) {
    if (!n) continue;
    if (hay.includes(n)) score += 1;
  }
  return score;
}

// Rank by (1) score, (2) rating desc, (3) createdAt desc if present
const ranked = all
  .filter((r: any) => !excludeSlug || r.slug !== excludeSlug)
  .map((r: any) => ({ ...r, _score: scoreReview(r) }))
  .sort((a: any, b: any) => {
    if (b._score !== a._score) return b._score - a._score;
    const ar = Number.isFinite(+a.rating) ? +a.rating : -1;
    const br = Number.isFinite(+b.rating) ? +b.rating : -1;
    if (br !== ar) return br - ar;
    const ad = new Date(a.createdAt || 0).getTime();
    const bd = new Date(b.createdAt || 0).getTime();
    return bd - ad;
  })
  .slice(0, limit);

const hasData = ranked.length > 0;
---

{hasData && (
  <section class="related-reviews" aria-labelledby="related-reviews-title">
    <div class="container">
      <header class="section-head">
        <h2 id="related-reviews-title">{title}</h2>
        <p class="muted">
          Explore hands-on reviews for <strong>Teen Patti</strong>, <strong>Rummy</strong>, and more on <strong>Starsuu7</strong> (aka <strong>UU7</strong> • <strong>777</strong>).
        </p>
      </header>

      <div class="grid">
        {ranked.map((r: any) => {
          const href = `/reviews/${r.slug}`;
          const img = abs(r.image);
          const stars = Number.isFinite(+r.rating) ? Math.max(0, Math.min(5, Math.round(+r.rating))) : 0;

          return (
            <article class="review-card">
              <a href={href} class="image-link" aria-label={`Read review: ${r.title}`}>
                {img && <img class="cover" src={img} alt="" width="480" height="300" loading="lazy" />}
                {stars > 0 && <span class="rating" aria-label={`${stars} out of 5`}>{'★'.repeat(stars)}{'☆'.repeat(5 - stars)}</span>}
              </a>
              <div class="content">
                <h3 class="title"><a href={href}>{r.title}</a></h3>
                {r.gameName && <p class="meta"><strong>Game:</strong> {r.gameName}</p>}
                {r.excerpt && <p class="excerpt">{r.excerpt}</p>}
                <a class="cta" href={href} aria-label={`Read full review: ${r.title}`}>Read full review</a>
              </div>
            </article>
          );
        })}
      </div>

      {showCTA && (
        <div class="more-cta">
          <a class="btn" href="/reviews/" aria-label="See all reviews on Starsuu7">
            See all reviews
          </a>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  </section>
)}

// ===== src/components/SeoHead.astro =====

---
export interface Alternate {
  href: string;
  hreflang: string;
}

export interface Props {
  title: string;
  description: string;
  canonical: string;

  // OpenGraph / Twitter
  image?: string;
  imageAlt?: string;
  type?: 'website' | 'article'; // <- narrowed union
  locale?: string;              // e.g., 'en_IN'
  twitter?: string;             // handle like '@starsuu7'
  modifiedTime?: string;        // ISO 8601

  // SEO
  keywords?: string[];          // we still output <meta name="keywords"> (for your workflow)
  alternates?: Alternate[];
  noindex?: boolean;

  // Structured data (raw blocks)
  schemas?: any[];
}

const {
  title,
  description,
  canonical,
  image = '/wordpress/STARSUU7-Game.webp',
  imageAlt = 'Starsuu7 — Teen Patti & Rummy',
  type = 'website',                 // <- default safe literal
  locale = 'en_IN',
  twitter = '@starsuu7',
  modifiedTime,
  keywords = ['starsuu7', 'starsuu7 apk', 'starsuu7 download', 'teen patti app', 'rummy app', 'uu7', '777'],
  alternates = [{ href: canonical, hreflang: 'en-IN' }, { href: canonical, hreflang: 'x-default' }],
  noindex = false,
  schemas = []
} = Astro.props as Props;

const robots = noindex
  ? 'noindex,follow,max-snippet:-1,max-image-preview:large,max-video-preview:-1'
  : 'index,follow,max-snippet:-1,max-image-preview:large,max-video-preview:-1';
---

<title>{title}</title>
<meta name="description" content={description} />
<meta name="robots" content={robots} />
<meta name="googlebot" content={noindex ? 'noindex,follow' : 'index,follow'} />

<link rel="canonical" href={canonical} />
{alternates.map((alt) => <link rel="alternate" hreflang={alt.hreflang} href={alt.href} />)}

<meta name="keywords" content={keywords.join(', ')} />

<!-- Open Graph -->
<meta property="og:site_name" content="Starsuu7" />
<meta property="og:type" content={type} />
<meta property="og:locale" content={locale} />
<meta property="og:title" content={title} />
<meta property="og:description" content={description} />
<meta property="og:url" content={canonical} />
<meta property="og:image" content={image} />
<meta property="og:image:alt" content={imageAlt} />
{modifiedTime && <meta property="og:updated_time" content={modifiedTime} />}

<!-- Twitter -->
<meta name="twitter:card" content="summary_large_image" />
<meta name="twitter:title" content={title} />
<meta name="twitter:description" content={description} />
<meta name="twitter:image" content={image} />
<meta name="twitter:site" content={twitter} />

<meta name="theme-color" content="#100F14" />

{schemas.map((block) => (
  <script type="application/ld+json">{JSON.stringify(block)}</script>
))}

// ===== src/components/SidebarPromos.astro =====

import { getPromotions } from '../services/api';
import type { Promotion } from '../services/api';
import type { Locale } from '../i18n';
import { createPath } from '../lib/paths';

interface Props {
  limit?: number;
  lang?: Locale;
}
const { limit = 3, lang = 'en' } = Astro.props;

const promos = await getPromotions(lang);
const recent = promos.filter(p => p.imageUrl).slice(0, limit);

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const toAbsolute = (p?: string) => !p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : new URL(p, API_BASE_URL).toString());
---
{recent.length > 0 && (
  <div class="sidebar-widget">
    <h3 class="widget-title">Latest Promotions</h3>
    <div class="promo-list">
      {recent.map((promo: Promotion) => (
        <a href={createPath(`/promotions/${promo.slug}/`, lang)} class="promo-item">

import { getBlogPosts } from '../services/api';

  lang?: Locale;
}

const allPosts = await getBlogPosts(lang);
const allTags = allPosts.flatMap(post => post.tags);

const tagCounts = allTags.reduce((acc, tag) => {
  acc[tag] = (acc[tag] || 0) + 1;
  return acc;
}, {} as Record<string, number>);

const popularTags = Object.entries(tagCounts)
  .sort(([, a], [, b]) => b - a)
  .slice(0, 15)
  .map(([tag]) => tag);

<script>
  // Script remains unchanged
  const wrapper = document.querySelector('.testimonial-carousel-wrapper') as HTMLElement | null;
  if (wrapper) {
    const grid = wrapper.querySelector('.grid') as HTMLElement | null;
    const dotsContainer = wrapper.querySelector('.dots') as HTMLElement | null;
    const cards = Array.from(wrapper.querySelectorAll('.testimonial-card')) as HTMLElement[];
    if (grid && dotsContainer && cards.length > 0 && window.matchMedia("(max-width: 767px)").matches) {
      cards.forEach((_, i) => {
        const button = document.createElement('button');
        button.setAttribute('aria-label', `Go to testimonial ${i + 1}`);
        button.addEventListener('click', () => {
          const cardWidth = cards[0].offsetWidth;
          const gap = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(grid).gap);
          grid.scrollTo({
            left: i * (cardWidth + gap),
            behavior: 'smooth'
          });
        });
        dotsContainer.appendChild(button);
      });
      const dots = Array.from(dotsContainer.querySelectorAll('button'));
      if (dots.length > 0) {
        dots[0].classList.add('is-active');
      }
      const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        entries.forEach(entry => {
          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
            const index = cards.indexOf(entry.target as HTMLElement);
            dots.forEach(dot => dot.classList.remove('is-active'));
            if (dots[index]) {
              dots[index].classList.add('is-active');
            }
          }
        });
      }, { root: grid, threshold: 0.6 });
      cards.forEach(card => observer.observe(card));
    }
  }
</script>

// ===== src/i18n.ts =====

// ===== src/i18n.ts =====
// --- FINALIZED: Enforces trailing slashes on all generated paths ---

export const defaultLocale = 'en';
export const locales = ['en', 'hi'] as const;
export type Locale = typeof locales[number];

/**
 * Ensures a path ends with a trailing slash.
 * Root path '/' is left as is.
 * @param path The path to check.
 * @returns The path with a trailing slash.
 */
function ensureTrailingSlash(path: string): string {
  if (path.length > 1 && !path.endsWith('/')) {
    return `${path}/`;
  }
  return path;
}

/**
 * Creates a language-aware path with a guaranteed trailing slash.
 * @param path The base path (e.g., '/faq' or '/faq/').
 * @param locale The target locale.
 * @returns The fully-qualified, language-aware path with a trailing slash (e.g., '/hi/faq/').
 */
export function createPath(path: string, locale: Locale): string {
  // Normalize base path to not have a leading slash for joining
  const basePath = path.startsWith('/') ? path.substring(1) : path;
  
  // Remove trailing slash for consistent joining
  const cleanBasePath = basePath.endsWith('/') ? basePath.slice(0, -1) : basePath;

  let finalPath: string;

  if (locale === defaultLocale) {
    finalPath = `/${cleanBasePath}`;
  } else {
    finalPath = `/${locale}/${cleanBasePath}`;
  }

  // Ensure trailing slash on all paths, including root for other languages (e.g., /hi/)
  return ensureTrailingSlash(finalPath);
}


/**
 * Strips the trailing slash from a path, unless it's the root path '/'.
 * @param path The path to strip.
 * @returns Path without a trailing slash.
 */
function stripTrailingSlash(path: string) {
  if (path.length > 1 && path.endsWith('/')) return path.slice(0, -1);
  return path;
}

/**
 * Splits a pathname into its parts, handling leading slashes consistently.
 * @param pathname The URL pathname.
 * @returns An array of path segments.
 */
function splitPath(pathname: string) {
  const clean = stripTrailingSlash(pathname);
  return clean.startsWith('/') ? clean.split('/') : `/${clean}`.split('/');
}

/**
 * Extracts the locale from a URL pathname.
 * @param pathname The URL pathname.
 * @returns The detected locale or the default locale.
 */
export function getLocaleFromPath(pathname: string): Locale {
  const parts = splitPath(pathname);
  const maybe = parts[1];
  return (locales as readonly string[]).includes(maybe) ? (maybe as Locale) : defaultLocale;
}

/**
 * Gets the part of the path *after* the locale prefix.
 * @param pathname The URL pathname.
 * @returns The path without the locale prefix (e.g., '/blog/my-post').
 */
export function getPathWithoutLocale(pathname: string): string {
  const parts = splitPath(pathname);
  const current = getLocaleFromPath(pathname);
  const hasPrefix = parts[1] === current;

  let rest = '/';
  if (hasPrefix) {
    const remainder = parts.slice(2).join('/');
    rest = remainder ? `/${remainder}` : '/';
  } else {
    rest = parts.slice(1).join('/');
    rest = rest ? `/${rest}` : '/';
  }
  // This function should return the canonical non-slashed path for lookup
  return stripTrailingSlash(rest) || '/';
}

/**
 * Builds the correct, slash-terminated path for a given target locale.
 * @param target The target locale.
 * @param pathname The current page's pathname.
 * @returns The new path with the correct locale prefix and trailing slash.
 */
export function buildLocalePath(target: Locale, pathname: string): string {
  const rest = getPathWithoutLocale(pathname);
  return createPath(rest, target);
}

/**
 * A hook-like function to get i18n utilities within an Astro component.
 * @param Astro The global Astro object.
 * @returns An object with the current locale and a path builder function.
 */
export function useI18n(Astro: { url: URL }) {
  const pathname = Astro.url.pathname;
  const locale = getLocaleFromPath(pathname);

  return {
    locale,
    locales: locales as readonly Locale[],
    getLocalePath: (target: Locale) => buildLocalePath(target, pathname),
    getPathWithoutLocale, // Exposing this for Base.astro
  };
}

<!DOCTYPE html>

      (function () {
        const portal = document.getElementById('global-mobile-menu');
        const sheet = portal && portal.querySelector('.gmm-sheet');
        const focusablesSel = 'button, [href], input, select, textarea, [tabindex]:not([tabindex="-1"])';
        let lastActive = null;
        function trapFocus(e) {
          if (!portal || portal.getAttribute('aria-hidden') === 'true') return;
          const nodes = sheet ? sheet.querySelectorAll(focusablesSel) : [];
          const first = nodes[0];
          const last = nodes[nodes.length - 1];
          if (!first || !last) return;
          if (e.key === 'Tab') {
            if (e.shiftKey && document.activeElement === first) { e.preventDefault(); last.focus(); } 
            else if (!e.shiftKey && document.activeElement === last) { e.preventDefault(); first.focus(); }
          } else if (e.key === 'Escape') {
            e.preventDefault();
            if (window.AppMenu && typeof window.AppMenu.close === 'function') window.AppMenu.close();
          }
        }
        function openMenu() {
          if (!portal) return;
          lastActive = document.activeElement || null;
          portal.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
          document.documentElement.style.overflow = 'hidden';
          document.body.style.touchAction = 'none';
          if (sheet && typeof sheet.focus === 'function') sheet.focus();
          document.addEventListener('keydown', trapFocus);
        }
        function closeMenu() {
          if (!portal) return;
          portal.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
          document.documentElement.style.overflow = '';
          document.body.style.touchAction = '';
          document.removeEventListener('keydown', trapFocus);
          try {
            if (lastActive && 'focus' in lastActive && typeof lastActive.focus === 'function') {
              (lastActive).focus();
            }
          } catch (_) {}
        }
        window.AppMenu = { open: openMenu, close: closeMenu, toggle: () => (portal && portal.getAttribute('aria-hidden') === 'true' ? openMenu() : closeMenu()) };
        window.addEventListener('open-global-menu', () => openMenu());
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
          const t = e.target;
          if (!(t instanceof Element)) return;
          if (t.closest('[data-gmm-close]')) { e.preventDefault(); closeMenu(); }
          if (t.closest('[data-gmm-link]')) { closeMenu(); }

          window.removeEventListener('keydown', onFirstIntent);
          window.removeEventListener('scroll', onFirstIntent, { passive: true });

// ===== src/lib/i18n.ts =====

import type { Locale } from "../i18n";

const translations = import.meta.glob<{ default: Record<string, any> }>('/src/locales/*.json', { eager: true });

/**
 * Returns a translation function `t` for the specified locale.
 *
 * @param lang The desired locale ('en' or 'hi').
 * @returns A function `t(key: string)` that returns the translated value (string, array, object).
 */
export function useTranslations(lang: Locale) {
  const langPath = `/src/locales/${lang}.json`;
  const dict = translations[langPath]?.default ?? translations['/src/locales/en.json'].default;

  /**
   * --- UPDATED: Uses a more robust 'reduce' method to traverse the object path. ---
   * This correctly handles nested objects and arrays.
   */
  return function t(key: string): any {
    const result = key.split('.').reduce((obj, currentKey) => {
      // Check if the current object is valid and has the key
      if (obj && typeof obj === 'object' && currentKey in obj) {
        return obj[currentKey as keyof typeof obj];
      }
      // If the path is broken at any point, return undefined
      return undefined;
    }, dict as any);

    // If the lookup failed, return the original key as a fallback for debugging.
    // Otherwise, return the found value.
    return result === undefined ? key : result;
  };
}

// ===== src/lib/ld.ts =====

/**
 * src/lib/ld.ts
 * Lightweight JSON-LD factory helpers for Starsuu7.
 *
 * All factories return plain JS objects you can pass to <SeoHead schemas={[ ... ]} />.
 *
 * Usage:
 *   import * as LD from '@/lib/ld';
 *   const schemas = [
 *     LD.makeOrganization({ name: 'Starsuu7', url: base, logo: '/logo.webp' }, base),
 *     LD.makeWebSite({ name: 'Starsuu7', url: base, hasSearch: true }, base),
 *     LD.makeWebPage({ name: pageTitle, description, url: canonical }, base),
 *     LD.makeMobileApp({ name: 'Starsuu7', downloadUrl, version, fileSize, dateModified }, base),
 *     LD.makeBreadcrumb([{ name: 'Home', item: '/' }, { name: 'FAQ', item: '/faq' }], base),
 *     LD.makeFAQ([{ q:'How to play Teen Patti?', a:'...' }])
 *   ];
 */

type MaybeDate = string | Date | undefined;

export type OrgInput = {
  name: string;
  url: string;          // absolute or relative
  logo?: string;        // absolute or relative
  sameAs?: string[];    // social profiles
  inLanguage?: string;  // e.g., 'en-IN'
};

export type WebSiteInput = {
  name: string;
  url: string;              // absolute or relative
  inLanguage?: string;
  hasSearch?: boolean;
  searchPath?: string;      // defaults to '/search?q={search_term_string}'
};

export type WebPageInput = {
  name: string;
  description?: string;
  url: string;              // absolute or relative
  inLanguage?: string;
  isPartOf?: { name: string; url: string };
};

export type MobileAppInput = {
  name: string;             // app name
  downloadUrl: string;      // absolute or relative
  version?: string;         // e.g. '1.0.0'
  fileSize?: string;        // e.g. '22.1 MB'
  dateModified?: MaybeDate; // ISO or parseable
  operatingSystem?: string; // default 'Android'
  category?: string;        // default 'GameApplication'
  image?: string;           // logo/cover
  offers?: {
    price?: string;         // '0'
    priceCurrency?: string; // 'INR'
    availability?: string;  // https://schema.org/InStock
  };
  publisher?: {
    name: string;
    url: string;
    logo?: string;
  };
  inLanguage?: string;
};

export type SoftwareAppInput = MobileAppInput & {
  // Optional variation for SoftwareApplication (non-mobile)
  applicationCategory?: string; // e.g. 'GameApplication'|'BusinessApplication'
};

export type FAQItem = { q: string; a: string };
export type BreadcrumbItem = { name: string; item: string };

export type ArticleInput = {
  headline: string;
  description?: string;
  url: string;
  image?: string | string[];
  author?: { name: string } | { name: string }[];
  publisher?: { name: string; logo?: string };
  datePublished?: MaybeDate;
  dateModified?: MaybeDate;
  inLanguage?: string;
};

const DEFAULT_LANG = 'en-IN';

/* ----------------------------- helpers ---------------------------------- */

function ensureAbsoluteUrl(urlOrPath?: string, base?: string): string | undefined {
  if (!urlOrPath) return undefined;
  try {
    // Already absolute
    if (/^https?:\/\//i.test(urlOrPath)) return urlOrPath;
    if (!base) return urlOrPath; // fallback to given
    return new URL(urlOrPath, base).toString();
  } catch {
    return urlOrPath;
  }
}

function toISO(d?: MaybeDate): string | undefined {
  if (!d) return undefined;
  try {
    const dt = typeof d === 'string' ? new Date(d) : d;
    return isNaN(dt.getTime()) ? undefined : dt.toISOString();
  } catch {
    return undefined;
  }
}

function stripHtml(s?: string): string | undefined {
  if (!s) return s;
  return s.replace(/<[^>]*>/g, '').trim();
}

/* ------------------------------ factories -------------------------------- */

/** Organization */
export function makeOrganization(input: OrgInput, base?: string) {
  const url = ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.url, base);
  const logo = ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.logo, base);
  const obj: any = {
    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
    '@type': 'Organization',
    name: input.name,
    url,
    inLanguage: input.inLanguage || DEFAULT_LANG
  };
  if (logo) obj.logo = { '@type': 'ImageObject', url: logo };
  if (input.sameAs?.length) obj.sameAs = input.sameAs;
  return obj;
}

/** WebSite (with optional SearchAction) */
export function makeWebSite(input: WebSiteInput, base?: string) {
  const url = ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.url, base);
  const obj: any = {
    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
    '@type': 'WebSite',
    name: input.name,
    url,
    inLanguage: input.inLanguage || DEFAULT_LANG
  };
  if (input.hasSearch) {
    const searchTarget = ensureAbsoluteUrl(
      input.searchPath || '/search?q={search_term_string}',
      url
    );
    obj.potentialAction = {
      '@type': 'SearchAction',
      target: searchTarget,
      'query-input': 'required name=search_term_string'
    };
  }
  return obj;
}

/** WebPage */
export function makeWebPage(input: WebPageInput, base?: string) {
  const url = ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.url, base);
  const obj: any = {
    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
    '@type': 'WebPage',
    name: input.name,
    url,
    inLanguage: input.inLanguage || DEFAULT_LANG
  };
  if (input.description) obj.description = stripHtml(input.description);
  if (input.isPartOf) {
    obj.isPartOf = {
      '@type': 'WebSite',
      name: input.isPartOf.name,
      url: ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.isPartOf.url, base)
    };
  }
  return obj;
}

/** MobileApplication (Android default) */
export function makeMobileApp(input: MobileAppInput, base?: string) {
  const downloadUrl = ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.downloadUrl, base);
  const image = ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.image, base);
  const publisherUrl = ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.publisher?.url, base);
  const publisherLogo = ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.publisher?.logo, base);

  const obj: any = {
    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
    '@type': 'MobileApplication',
    name: input.name,
    operatingSystem: input.operatingSystem || 'Android',
    applicationCategory: input.category || 'GameApplication',
    inLanguage: input.inLanguage || DEFAULT_LANG,
    url: ensureAbsoluteUrl('/', base),
    downloadUrl,
    softwareVersion: input.version,
    fileSize: input.fileSize,
    dateModified: toISO(input.dateModified)
  };
  if (image) obj.image = image;
  if (input.offers) {
    obj.offers = {
      '@type': 'Offer',
      price: input.offers.price ?? '0',
      priceCurrency: input.offers.priceCurrency ?? 'INR',
      availability: input.offers.availability ?? 'https://schema.org/InStock',
      url: downloadUrl
    };
  }
  if (input.publisher) {
    obj.publisher = {
      '@type': 'Organization',
      name: input.publisher.name,
      url: publisherUrl
    };
    if (publisherLogo) {
      obj.publisher.logo = { '@type': 'ImageObject', url: publisherLogo };
    }
  }
  return obj;
}

/** SoftwareApplication (generic app, non-mobile) */
export function makeSoftwareApplication(input: SoftwareAppInput, base?: string) {
  const downloadUrl = ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.downloadUrl, base);
  const image = ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.image, base);
  const obj: any = {
    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
    '@type': 'SoftwareApplication',
    name: input.name,
    applicationCategory: input.applicationCategory || input.category || 'GameApplication',
    operatingSystem: input.operatingSystem || 'Android',
    inLanguage: input.inLanguage || DEFAULT_LANG,
    url: ensureAbsoluteUrl('/', base),
    downloadUrl,
    softwareVersion: input.version,
    fileSize: input.fileSize,
    dateModified: toISO(input.dateModified)
  };
  if (image) obj.image = image;
  return obj;
}

/** FAQPage items; embed array inside your page as a separate schema if you like */
export function makeFAQ(items: FAQItem[]) {
  return {
    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
    '@type': 'FAQPage',
    mainEntity: items.map(({ q, a }) => ({
      '@type': 'Question',
      name: q,
      acceptedAnswer: { '@type': 'Answer', text: stripHtml(a) }
    }))
  };
}

/** BreadcrumbList */
export function makeBreadcrumb(items: BreadcrumbItem[], base?: string) {
  return {
    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
    '@type': 'BreadcrumbList',
    itemListElement: items.map((it, i) => ({
      '@type': 'ListItem',
      position: i + 1,
      name: it.name,
      item: ensureAbsoluteUrl(it.item, base)
    }))
  };
}

/** Article (for blog/news pages if/when you add them) */
export function makeArticle(input: ArticleInput, base?: string) {
  const url = ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.url, base);
  const image = Array.isArray(input.image)
    ? input.image.map((i) => ensureAbsoluteUrl(i, base))
    : ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.image, base);
  const obj: any = {
    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
    '@type': 'Article',
    headline: input.headline,
    description: stripHtml(input.description),
    url,
    inLanguage: input.inLanguage || DEFAULT_LANG,
    datePublished: toISO(input.datePublished),
    dateModified: toISO(input.dateModified)
  };
  if (image) obj.image = image;
  if (input.author) obj.author = input.author;
  if (input.publisher) {
    obj.publisher = {
      '@type': 'Organization',
      name: input.publisher.name
    };
    if (input.publisher.logo) {
      obj.publisher.logo = {
        '@type': 'ImageObject',
        url: ensureAbsoluteUrl(input.publisher.logo, base)
      };
    }
  }
  return obj;
}


// ===== src/lib/paths.ts =====

// ===== src/lib/paths.ts =====
// --- UPDATED: Slugify function is now Unicode-aware ---
import { defaultLocale, type Locale } from '../i18n';

export function createPath(path: string, locale: Locale): string {
  if (!path.startsWith('/')) {
    path = `/${path}`;
  }
  if (locale === defaultLocale) {
    return path;
  }
  const finalPath = `/${locale}${path === '/' ? '' : path}`;
  return finalPath;
}

/**
 * Creates a URL-friendly "slug" from a given string, now with Unicode support.
 */
export function slugify(text: string): string {
  if (!text) return '';
  
  const a = 'àáâäæãåāăąçćčđďèéêëēėęěğǵḧîïíīįìłḿñńǹňôöòóœøōõőṕŕřßśšşșťțûüùúūǘůűųẃẍÿýžźż·/_,:;'
  const b = 'aaaaaaaaaacccddeeeeeeeegghiiiiiilmnnnnoooooooooprrsssssttuuuuuuuuuwxyyzzz------'
  const p = new RegExp(a.split('').join('|'), 'g')

  return text.toString().toLowerCase()
    .replace(/\s+/g, '-') // Replace spaces with -
    .replace(p, c => b.charAt(a.indexOf(c))) // Replace special characters
    .replace(/&/g, '-and-') // Replace & with 'and'
    .replace(/[^\w-]+/g, '') // Remove all non-word chars
    .replace(/--+/g, '-') // Replace multiple - with single -
    .replace(/^-+/, '') // Trim - from start of text
    .replace(/-+$/, '') // Trim - from end of text
}
