// ===== src/pages/api/rebuild-now.ts =====

import type { APIRoute } from 'astro';
import { exec } from 'node:child_process';
import { promisify } from 'node:util';

const execPromise = promisify(exec);

// Get the secret token from your environment variables
const REBUILD_SECRET = import.meta.env.REBUILD_SECRET_TOKEN;

export const GET: APIRoute = async ({ request }) => {
  if (!REBUILD_SECRET) {
    console.error("REBUILD_SECRET_TOKEN is not set in the environment.");
    return new Response('Server not configured for rebuilds.', { status: 500 });
  }

  // Get the secret from the request URL (e.g., /api/rebuild-now?secret=YOUR_TOKEN)
  const url = new URL(request.url);
  const secret = url.searchParams.get('secret');

  // 1. Check if the secret token is valid
  if (secret !== REBUILD_SECRET) {
    return new Response('Invalid secret token.', { status: 401 });
  }

  // 2. Run the build command
  try {
    console.log("Rebuild request received. Starting `npm run build`...");

    // Execute the build command from the root of your Astro project
    const { stdout, stderr } = await execPromise('npm run build', {
      // Set the working directory to the project root
      cwd: process.cwd(), 
    });

    console.log("Astro build successful.");
    console.log("STDOUT:", stdout);
    if (stderr) {
      console.warn("STDERR:", stderr);
    }

    // 3. Send a success response
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({
      message: 'Build triggered successfully.',
      output: stdout,
    }), {
      status: 200,
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    });

  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Error during rebuild:", error);
    // 4. Send an error response
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ message: 'Build failed.', error: error.message }), {
      status: 500,
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    });
  }
};

// ===== src/pages/blog/author/[author].astro =====

---
// ===== src/pages/blog/author/[author].astro =====
// --- CORRECTED: Now parses Markdown in excerpts ---
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../../components/Footer.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { getBlogPosts } from '../../../services/api';
import type { BlogPostListItem } from '../../../services/api';
import { slugify } from '../../../lib/paths';

// This is now an SSR page, so getStaticPaths is removed.

const locale: 'en' = 'en';
const { author: authorSlug } = Astro.params;

const allPosts = await getBlogPosts(locale);

const filteredPosts = allPosts.filter(p => slugify(p.author) === authorSlug);

const authorName = filteredPosts.length > 0 ? filteredPosts[0].author : authorSlug;

const pageTitle = `Posts by ${authorName} | Starsuu7 Blog`;
const pageDescription = `Read all articles written by ${authorName} on the Starsuu7 blog.`;
const h1 = `Author: ${authorName}`;
const canonical = new URL(`/blog/author/${authorSlug}/`, Astro.site).toString();

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const toAbsolute = (p?: string) => !p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : new URL(p, API_BASE_URL).toString());
const formatDate = (date: string) => new Date(date).toLocaleDateString('en-US', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
---

<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDescription} canonical={canonical} lang={locale}>
  <div class="desktop-layout"><Header lang={locale} /></div>
  <div class="mobile-layout"><MobileAppShell title={h1} active="blog" lang={locale} showBack={true} /></div>

  <main class="blog-archive-page">
    <div class="container">
      <header class="page-header">
        <p class="archive-type">Blog Archive</p>
        <h1>{h1}</h1>
      </header>

      {filteredPosts.length > 0 ? (
        <div class="post-grid">
          {filteredPosts.map(async (post: BlogPostListItem) => {
            const postUrl = `/blog/${post.slug}/`;
            return (
              <article class="post-card">
                <a href={postUrl} class="card-image-link" aria-label={`Read: ${post.title}`}>
                  <img src={toAbsolute(post.image)} alt={`Featured image for ${post.title}`} loading="lazy" width="400" height="250" class="card-image" />
                </a>
                <div class="card-content">
                  <p class="card-meta"><time datetime={post.publishedAt}>{formatDate(post.publishedAt)}</time></p>
                  <h2 class="card-title"><a href={postUrl}>{post.title}</a></h2>
                  <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(post.excerpt || '')} />
                </div>
              </article>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      ) : (
        <p>No posts found for this author.</p>
      )}
    </div>
  </main>

  <Footer lang={locale} />
</Base>

// ===== src/pages/blog/category/[category].astro =====

---
// ===== src/pages/blog/category/[category].astro =====
// --- CORRECTED: Now parses Markdown in excerpts ---
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../../components/Footer.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { getBlogPosts } from '../../../services/api';
import type { BlogPostListItem } from '../../../services/api';
import { slugify } from '../../../lib/paths';

export async function getStaticPaths() {
  const posts = await getBlogPosts('en');
  const uniqueCategories = [...new Set(posts.map(post => post.tags[0]).filter(Boolean))];
  
  return uniqueCategories.map(category => ({
    params: { category: slugify(category) },
  }));
}

const locale: 'en' = 'en';
const { category } = Astro.params;

const allPosts = await getBlogPosts(locale);

const filteredPosts = allPosts.filter(post => {
  const postCategory = post.tags[0];
  return postCategory && slugify(postCategory) === category;
});

const categoryName = filteredPosts.length > 0 ? filteredPosts[0].tags[0] : category;

const pageTitle = `"${categoryName}" Category | Starsuu7 Blog`;
const pageDescription = `Browse all articles in the "${categoryName}" category on the official Starsuu7 blog.`;
const h1 = `Category: ${categoryName}`;
const canonical = new URL(`/blog/category/${category}/`, Astro.site).toString();

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const toAbsolute = (p?: string) => !p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : new URL(p, API_BASE_URL).toString());
const formatDate = (date: string) => new Date(date).toLocaleDateString('en-IN', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
---

  <main class="blog-archive-page">
    <div class="container">
      <header class="page-header">
        <p class="archive-type">Blog Archive</p>

      </header>

      {filteredPosts.length > 0 ? (
        <div class="post-grid">
          {filteredPosts.map(async (post: BlogPostListItem) => {
            const postUrl = `/blog/${post.slug}/`;
            return (
              <article class="post-card">
                <a href={postUrl} class="card-image-link" aria-label={`Read: ${post.title}`}>
                  <img src={toAbsolute(post.image)} alt={`Featured image for ${post.title}`} loading="lazy" width="400" height="250" class="card-image" />
                </a>
                <div class="card-content">
                  <p class="card-meta"><time datetime={post.publishedAt}>{formatDate(post.publishedAt)}</time></p>
                  <h2 class="card-title"><a href={postUrl}>{post.title}</a></h2>
                  <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(post.excerpt || '')} />
                </div>
              </article>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      ) : (
        <p>No posts found in this category.</p>
      )}
    </div>
  </main>
  
  <Footer lang={locale} />
</Base>

  @media (max-width: 767px) { .blog-archive-page { padding-block: 24px; } .mobile-layout + .blog-archive-page { padding-top: 0; } }
  .page-header { text-align: center; margin-bottom: 36px; }

  .post-card:hover { transform: translateY(-6px); box-shadow: var(--shadow-lg); }

// --- CORRECTED: Parses Markdown in excerpts & restores excerpt in grid view ---
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../components/Footer.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { getBlogPosts } from '../../services/api';
import type { BlogPostListItem } from '../../services/api';
import { useTranslations } from '../../lib/i18n';
import type { Locale } from '../../i18n';

const locale: Locale = 'en';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

const POSTS_PER_PAGE = Number(import.meta.env.PUBLIC_POSTS_PER_PAGE || 13);
const allPosts = await getBlogPosts(locale);

const heroPost = allPosts.length > 0 ? allPosts[0] : null;
const otherPosts = allPosts.slice(1, POSTS_PER_PAGE);

const totalPages = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(allPosts.length / POSTS_PER_PAGE));

const pageTitle = t('blogIndex.title');
const pageDescription = t('blogIndex.description');
const h1 = t('blogIndex.h1');
const subheading = t('blogIndex.subheading');

const canonical = new URL('/blog/', Astro.site).toString();
const nextUrl = totalPages > 1 ? new URL('/blog/page/2/', Astro.site).toString() : undefined;
const rssUrl = new URL('/rss.xml', Astro.site).toString();

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const toAbsolute = (p?: string) => !p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : new URL(p, API_BASE_URL).toString());

const formatDate = (date: string) => new Date(date).toLocaleDateString('en-IN', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
---

<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDescription} canonical={canonical} nextUrl={nextUrl} rssUrl={rssUrl} lang={locale}>
  
  <div class="desktop-layout">
    <Header lang={locale} />
  </div>
  <div class="mobile-layout">
    <MobileAppShell title={h1} active="blog" lang={locale} />
  </div>

  <main class="blog-index-page">
    <div class="container">
      <header class="page-header">
        <h1>{h1}</h1>
        <p class="muted">{subheading}</p>
      </header>

      {heroPost && (
        <section class="hero-post-section" aria-labelledby="hero-post-title">
          <article class="hero-card">
            <div class="hero-image-wrapper">
              <a href={`/blog/${heroPost.slug}/`} aria-label={`Read more about ${heroPost.title}`}>
                <img src={toAbsolute(heroPost.image)} alt={`Featured image for ${heroPost.title}`} width="1200" height="600" loading="eager" />
              </a>
            </div>
            <div class="hero-content">
              <p class="hero-meta"><time datetime={heroPost.publishedAt}>{formatDate(heroPost.publishedAt)}</time></p>
              <h2 id="hero-post-title" class="hero-title"><a href={`/blog/${heroPost.slug}/`}>{heroPost.title}</a></h2>
              
              <!-- UPDATED: Use set:html to render parsed Markdown -->
              <div class="hero-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(heroPost.excerpt || '')} />

              <a href={`/blog/${heroPost.slug}/`} class="hero-cta">{t('recentBlogs.readMore')} &rarr;</a>
            </div>
          </article>
        </section>
      )}

      {otherPosts.length > 0 && (
        <section class="post-grid-section" aria-label="Older posts">
          <div class="post-grid">
            {otherPosts.map(async (post: BlogPostListItem) => {
              const postUrl = `/blog/${post.slug}/`;
              return (
                <article class="post-card">
                  <a href={postUrl} class="card-image-link" aria-label={`Read: ${post.title}`}>
                    <img src={toAbsolute(post.image)} alt={`Featured image for blog post: ${post.title}`} loading="lazy" width="400" height="250" class="card-image" />
                  </a>
                  <div class="card-content">
                    <p class="card-meta"><time datetime={post.publishedAt}>{formatDate(post.publishedAt)}</time></p>
                    <h3 class="card-title"><a href={postUrl}>{post.title}</a></h3>
                    
                    <!-- UPDATED: Use set:html to render parsed Markdown -->
                    <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(post.excerpt || '')} />
                  </div>
                </article>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </section>
      )}

      {totalPages > 1 && (
        <nav class="pager" aria-label="Blog pages">
          <ul>
            <li><span class="pg-btn" aria-disabled="true">{t('blogIndex.pager.prev')}</span></li>
            <li class="pg-status">{t('blogIndex.pager.pageStatus').replace('{currentPage}', '1').replace('{totalPages}', String(totalPages))}</li>
            <li><a class="pg-btn" href="/blog/page/2/" aria-label="Next page">{t('blogIndex.pager.next')}</a></li>
            <li class="desktop-layout"><a class="pg-btn" href={`/blog/page/${totalPages}/`} aria-label="Go to last page">{t('blogIndex.pager.last')}</a></li>
          </ul>
        </nav>
      )}
    </div>
  </main>
  
  <Footer lang={locale} />
</Base>

// ===== src/pages/blog/page/[page].astro =====

---
// ===== src/pages/blog/page/[page].astro =====
// --- CORRECTED: Parses Markdown in excerpts ---
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../../components/Footer.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { getBlogPosts } from '../../../services/api';
import type { BlogPostListItem } from '../../../services/api';
import { useTranslations } from '../../../lib/i18n';
import type { Locale } from '../../../i18n';

const locale: Locale = 'en';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

const { page } = Astro.params;
const blogRoot = '/blog/';

const POSTS_PER_PAGE = Number(import.meta.env.PUBLIC_POSTS_PER_PAGE || 9);
const CURRENT_PAGE = Number.parseInt(page ?? '1', 10);

const allPosts: BlogPostListItem[] = await getBlogPosts(locale);
const totalPages = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(allPosts.length / POSTS_PER_PAGE));

if (Number.isNaN(CURRENT_PAGE) || CURRENT_PAGE < 1) { return Astro.redirect(blogRoot); }
if (CURRENT_PAGE === 1) { return Astro.redirect(blogRoot); }
if (CURRENT_PAGE > totalPages && totalPages > 0) { return Astro.redirect(blogRoot + `page/${totalPages}/`); }

const start = (CURRENT_PAGE - 1) * POSTS_PER_PAGE;
const pagePosts = allPosts.slice(start, start + POSTS_PER_PAGE);

const canonical = new URL(blogRoot + `page/${CURRENT_PAGE}/`, Astro.site).toString();
const prevUrl = CURRENT_PAGE > 1 ? new URL(CURRENT_PAGE === 2 ? blogRoot : blogRoot + `page/${CURRENT_PAGE - 1}/`, Astro.site).toString() : undefined;
const nextUrl = CURRENT_PAGE < totalPages ? new URL(blogRoot + `page/${CURRENT_PAGE + 1}/`, Astro.site).toString() : undefined;

const pageTitle = t('blogPaginated.title').replace('{currentPage}', String(CURRENT_PAGE));
const pageDescription = t('blogPaginated.description');
const h1 = t('blogPaginated.h1');
const firstPageText = t('blogPaginated.firstPage');

const formatDate = (date: string) => new Date(date).toLocaleDateString('en-IN', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const toAbsolute = (p?: string) => !p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : new URL(p, API_BASE_URL).toString());
---
<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDescription} canonical={canonical} prevUrl={prevUrl} nextUrl={nextUrl} lang={locale}>

  <div class="desktop-layout">
    <Header lang={locale} />
  </div>
  <div class="mobile-layout">
    <MobileAppShell title={`${h1} - Page ${CURRENT_PAGE}`} active="blog" lang={locale} />
  </div>

  <main class="blog-index">
    <div class="container">
      <header class="section-head">
        <div>
          <h1>{h1}</h1>
          <p class="muted">{t('blogIndex.pager.pageStatus').replace('{currentPage}', String(CURRENT_PAGE)).replace('{totalPages}', String(totalPages))}</p>
        </div>
        <a href={blogRoot} class="btn-view-all" aria-label="Go to page 1">{firstPageText}</a>
      </header>

      {pagePosts.length === 0 ? ( <p class="muted">{t('blogPaginated.noPosts')}</p> ) : (
        <div class="post-grid">
          {pagePosts.map(async (post) => {
            const postUrl = blogRoot + `${post.slug}/`;
            return (
              <article class="post-card">
                <a href={postUrl} class="card-image-link" aria-label={`Read more: ${post.title}`}>
                  <img src={toAbsolute(post.image)} alt={`Featured image for blog post: ${post.title}`} loading="lazy" width="400" height="250" class="card-image"/>
                </a>
                <div class="card-content">
                  <p class="card-meta"><time datetime={post.publishedAt}>{formatDate(post.publishedAt)}</time></p>
                  <h2 class="card-title"><a href={postUrl}>{post.title}</a></h2>
                  
                  <!-- UPDATED: Use set:html to render parsed Markdown -->
                  <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(post.excerpt || '')} />
                </div>
              </article>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      )}

      <nav class="pager" aria-label="Pagination">
        <ul>
          <li class="desktop-layout"><a class="pg-btn" href={blogRoot} aria-label="Go to first page">« {firstPageText}</a></li>
          <li>{prevUrl ? (<a class="pg-btn" href={prevUrl} aria-label="Previous page">{t('blogIndex.pager.prev')}</a>) : (<span class="pg-btn" aria-disabled="true">{t('blogIndex.pager.prev')}</span>)}</li>
          <li class="pg-status" aria-current="page">{t('blogIndex.pager.pageStatus').replace('{currentPage}', String(CURRENT_PAGE)).replace('{totalPages}', String(totalPages))}</li>
          <li>{nextUrl ? (<a class="pg-btn" href={nextUrl} aria-label="Next page">{t('blogIndex.pager.next')}</a>) : (<span class="pg-btn" aria-disabled="true">{t('blogIndex.pager.next')}</span>)}</li>
          <li class="desktop-layout">{CURRENT_PAGE < totalPages ? (<a class="pg-btn" href={blogRoot + `page/${totalPages}/`} aria-label="Go to last page">{t('blogIndex.pager.last')}</a>) : (<span class="pg-btn" aria-disabled="true">{t('blogIndex.pager.last')}</span>)}</li>
        </ul>
      </nav>
    </div>
  </main>

  <Footer lang={locale} />
</Base>

  .mobile-layout { display: block; }
  @media (min-width: 768px) {

// ===== src/pages/blog/tag/[tag].astro =====

---
// ===== src/pages/blog/tag/[tag].astro =====
// --- CORRECTED: Now parses Markdown in excerpts ---
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../../components/Footer.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { getBlogPosts } from '../../../services/api';
import type { BlogPostListItem } from '../../../services/api';
import { slugify } from '../../../lib/paths';

export async function getStaticPaths() {
  const posts = await getBlogPosts('en');
  const uniqueTags = [...new Set(posts.flatMap(post => post.tags))];
  
  return uniqueTags.map(tag => ({
    params: { tag: slugify(tag) },
  }));
}

const locale: 'en' = 'en';
const { tag } = Astro.params;

const allPosts = await getBlogPosts(locale);

const filteredPosts = allPosts.filter(post => 
  post.tags.map(t => slugify(t)).includes(tag!)
);

const tagName = filteredPosts.length > 0 
  ? filteredPosts[0].tags.find(t => slugify(t) === tag) || tag
  : tag;

const pageTitle = `Posts tagged with "${tagName}" | Starsuu7 Blog`;
const pageDescription = `Find all blog posts and articles tagged with "${tagName}" on the official Starsuu7 blog.`;
const h1 = `Tag: ${tagName}`;
const canonical = new URL(`/blog/tag/${tag}/`, Astro.site).toString();

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const toAbsolute = (p?: string) => !p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : new URL(p, API_BASE_URL).toString());
const formatDate = (date: string) => new Date(date).toLocaleDateString('en-IN', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
---
<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDescription} canonical={canonical} lang={locale}>

  <div class="desktop-layout"><Header lang={locale} /></div>
  <div class="mobile-layout"><MobileAppShell title={h1} active="blog" lang={locale} showBack={true} /></div>

  <main class="blog-archive-page">
    <div class="container">
      <header class="page-header">
        <p class="archive-type">Blog Archive</p>
        <h1>{h1}</h1>
      </header>

      {filteredPosts.length > 0 ? (
        <div class="post-grid">
          {filteredPosts.map(async (post: BlogPostListItem) => {
            const postUrl = `/blog/${post.slug}/`;
            return (
              <article class="post-card">
                <a href={postUrl} class="card-image-link" aria-label={`Read: ${post.title}`}>
                  <img src={toAbsolute(post.image)} alt={`Featured image for ${post.title}`} loading="lazy" width="400" height="250" class="card-image" />
                </a>
                <div class="card-content">
                  <p class="card-meta"><time datetime={post.publishedAt}>{formatDate(post.publishedAt)}</time></p>
                  <h2 class="card-title"><a href={postUrl}>{post.title}</a></h2>
                  <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(post.excerpt || '')} />
                </div>
              </article>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      ) : (
        <p>No posts found for this tag.</p>
      )}
    </div>
  </main>
  
  <Footer lang={locale} />
</Base>

// ===== src/pages/hi/blog/author/[author].astro =====
// --- CORRECTED: Now parses Markdown in excerpts ---
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../../../components/Footer.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { getBlogPosts } from '../../../../services/api';
import type { BlogPostListItem } from '../../../../services/api';
import { slugify } from '../../../../lib/paths';

// This is an SSR page, getStaticPaths is removed.

const locale: 'hi' = 'hi';
const { author: authorSlug } = Astro.params;

const allPosts = await getBlogPosts(locale);

const filteredPosts = allPosts.filter(p => slugify(p.author) === authorSlug);

const authorName = filteredPosts.length > 0 ? filteredPosts[0].author : authorSlug;

const pageTitle = `${authorName} द्वारा पोस्ट | Starsuu7 ब्लॉग`;
const pageDescription = `Starsuu7 ब्लॉग पर ${authorName} द्वारा लिखे गए सभी ब्लॉग पोस्ट और लेख खोजें।`;
const h1 = `लेखक: ${authorName}`;
const canonical = new URL(`/hi/blog/author/${authorSlug}/`, Astro.site).toString();

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const toAbsolute = (p?: string) => !p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : new URL(p, API_BASE_URL).toString());
const formatDate = (date: string) => new Date(date).toLocaleDateString('hi-IN', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
---
<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDescription} canonical={canonical} lang={locale}>

  <div class="desktop-layout"><Header lang={locale} /></div>
  <div class="mobile-layout"><MobileAppShell title={h1} active="blog" lang={locale} showBack={true} /></div>

  <main class="blog-archive-page">
    <div class="container">
      <header class="page-header">
        <p class="archive-type">ब्लॉग आर्काइव</p>
        <h1>{h1}</h1>
      </header>

      {filteredPosts.length > 0 ? (
        <div class="post-grid">
          {filteredPosts.map(async (post: BlogPostListItem) => {
            const postUrl = `/hi/blog/${post.slug}/`;
            return (
              <article class="post-card">
                <a href={postUrl} class="card-image-link" aria-label={`पढ़ें: ${post.title}`}>
                  <img src={toAbsolute(post.image)} alt={`के लिए विशेष रुप से प्रदर्शित छवि ${post.title}`} loading="lazy" width="400" height="250" class="card-image" />
                </a>
                <div class="card-content">
                  <p class="card-meta"><time datetime={post.publishedAt}>{formatDate(post.publishedAt)}</time></p>
                  <h2 class="card-title"><a href={postUrl}>{post.title}</a></h2>
                  <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(post.excerpt || '')} />
                </div>
              </article>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      ) : (
        <p>इस लेखक के लिए कोई पोस्ट नहीं मिली।</p>
      )}
    </div>
  </main>
  
  <Footer lang={locale} />
</Base>

// ===== src/pages/hi/blog/category/[category].astro =====

// ===== src/pages/hi/blog/category/[category].astro =====
// --- CORRECTED: Now parses Markdown in excerpts ---
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../../../components/Footer.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { getBlogPosts } from '../../../../services/api';
import type { BlogPostListItem } from '../../../../services/api';
import { slugify } from '../../../../lib/paths';

// This page is now SSR, so getStaticPaths is removed.

const locale: 'hi' = 'hi';
const { category: categorySlug } = Astro.params;

const allPosts = await getBlogPosts(locale);

const filteredPosts = allPosts.filter(post => {
  const postCategory = post.tags[0];
  return postCategory && slugify(postCategory) === categorySlug;
});

const categoryName = filteredPosts.length > 0 ? filteredPosts[0].tags[0] : categorySlug;

const pageTitle = `"${categoryName}" श्रेणी | Starsuu7 ब्लॉग`;
const pageDescription = `Starsuu7 ब्लॉग पर "${categoryName}" श्रेणी के सभी लेख ब्राउज़ करें।`;
const h1 = `श्रेणी: ${categoryName}`;
const canonical = new URL(`/hi/blog/category/${categorySlug}/`, Astro.site).toString();

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const toAbsolute = (p?: string) => !p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : new URL(p, API_BASE_URL).toString());
const formatDate = (date: string) => new Date(date).toLocaleDateString('hi-IN', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
---
<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDescription} canonical={canonical} lang={locale}>

  <div class="desktop-layout"><Header lang={locale} /></div>
  <div class="mobile-layout"><MobileAppShell title={h1} active="blog" lang={locale} showBack={true} /></div>

  <main class="blog-archive-page">
    <div class="container">
      <header class="page-header">
        <p class="archive-type">ब्लॉग आर्काइव</p>
        <h1>{h1}</h1>
      </header>

      {filteredPosts.length > 0 ? (
        <div class="post-grid">
          {filteredPosts.map(async (post: BlogPostListItem) => {
            const postUrl = `/hi/blog/${post.slug}/`;
            return (
              <article class="post-card">
                <a href={postUrl} class="card-image-link" aria-label={`पढ़ें: ${post.title}`}>
                  <img src={toAbsolute(post.image)} alt={`के लिए विशेष रुप से प्रदर्शित छवि ${post.title}`} loading="lazy" width="400" height="250" class="card-image" />
                </a>
                <div class="card-content">
                  <p class="card-meta"><time datetime={post.publishedAt}>{formatDate(post.publishedAt)}</time></p>
                  <h2 class="card-title"><a href={postUrl}>{post.title}</a></h2>
                  <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(post.excerpt || '')} />
                </div>
              </article>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      ) : (
        <p>इस श्रेणी में कोई पोस्ट नहीं मिली।</p>
      )}
    </div>
  </main>
  
  <Footer lang={locale} />
</Base>

import { marked } from 'marked';

import { useTranslations } from '../../../lib/i18n';
import type { Locale } from '../../../i18n';

const locale: Locale = 'hi';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

const POSTS_PER_PAGE = Number(import.meta.env.PUBLIC_POSTS_PER_PAGE || 9);
const allPosts = await getBlogPosts(locale);

const heroPost = allPosts.length > 0 ? allPosts[0] : null;
const otherPosts = allPosts.slice(1, POSTS_PER_PAGE);

const totalPages = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(allPosts.length / POSTS_PER_PAGE));

const pageTitle = t('blogIndex.title');
const pageDescription = t('blogIndex.description');
const h1 = t('blogIndex.h1');
const subheading = t('blogIndex.subheading');

const canonical = new URL('/hi/blog/', Astro.site).toString();
const nextUrl = totalPages > 1 ? new URL('/hi/blog/page/2/', Astro.site).toString() : undefined;
const rssUrl = new URL('/rss.xml', Astro.site).toString();

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const toAbsolute = (p?: string) => !p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : new URL(p, API_BASE_URL).toString());

const formatDate = (date: string) => new Date(date).toLocaleDateString('hi-IN', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });

  </div>
  <div class="mobile-layout">
    <MobileAppShell title={h1} active="blog" lang={locale} />

    <div class="container">
      <header class="page-header">
        <h1>{h1}</h1>
        <p class="muted">{subheading}</p>
      </header>

      {heroPost && (
        <section class="hero-post-section" aria-labelledby="hero-post-title">
          <article class="hero-card">
            <div class="hero-image-wrapper">
              <a href={`/hi/blog/${heroPost.slug}/`} aria-label={`Read more about ${heroPost.title}`}>
                <img src={toAbsolute(heroPost.image)} alt={`Featured image for ${heroPost.title}`} width="1200" height="600" loading="eager" />
              </a>
            </div>
            <div class="hero-content">
              <p class="hero-meta"><time datetime={heroPost.publishedAt}>{formatDate(heroPost.publishedAt)}</time></p>
              <h2 id="hero-post-title" class="hero-title"><a href={`/hi/blog/${heroPost.slug}/`}>{heroPost.title}</a></h2>
              <div class="hero-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(heroPost.excerpt || '')} />
              <a href={`/hi/blog/${heroPost.slug}/`} class="hero-cta">{t('recentBlogs.readMore')} &rarr;</a>
            </div>
          </article>
        </section>
      )}

      {otherPosts.length > 0 && (
        <section class="post-grid-section" aria-label="Older posts">
          <div class="post-grid">
            {otherPosts.map(async (post: BlogPostListItem) => {
              const postUrl = `/hi/blog/${post.slug}/`;
              return (
                <article class="post-card">
                  <a href={postUrl} class="card-image-link" aria-label={`Read: ${post.title}`}>
                    <img src={toAbsolute(post.image)} alt={`Featured image for blog post: ${post.title}`} loading="lazy" width="400" height="250" class="card-image" />

                    <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(post.excerpt || '')} />
                  </div>
                </article>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </section>
      )}

      {totalPages > 1 && (
        <nav class="pager" aria-label="Blog pages">
          <ul>
            <li><span class="pg-btn" aria-disabled="true">{t('blogIndex.pager.prev')}</span></li>
            <li class="pg-status">{t('blogIndex.pager.pageStatus').replace('{currentPage}', '1').replace('{totalPages}', String(totalPages))}</li>
            <li><a class="pg-btn" href="/hi/blog/page/2/" aria-label="Next page">{t('blogIndex.pager.next')}</a></li>
            <li class="desktop-layout"><a class="pg-btn" href={`/hi/blog/page/${totalPages}/`} aria-label="Go to last page">{t('blogIndex.pager.last')}</a></li>
          </ul>
        </nav>
      )}
    </div>
  </main>
  
  <Footer lang={locale} />
</Base>

---
// ===== src/pages/hi/blog/page/[page].astro =====
// --- REFACTORED: Now uses a consistent grid layout and renders excerpts ---
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../../../components/Footer.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { getBlogPosts } from '../../../../services/api';
import type { BlogPostListItem } from '../../../../services/api';
import { useTranslations } from '../../../../lib/i18n';
import type { Locale } from '../../../../i18n';

// This page is now dynamically generated for any /hi/blog/page/... URL.
// We removed getStaticPaths.

const locale: Locale = 'hi';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

const { page } = Astro.params;
const blogRoot = '/hi/blog/'; // Hardcoded Hindi blog root

const POSTS_PER_PAGE = Number(import.meta.env.PUBLIC_POSTS_PER_PAGE || 9);
const CURRENT_PAGE = Number.parseInt(page ?? '1', 10);

const allPosts: BlogPostListItem[] = await getBlogPosts(locale);
const totalPages = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(allPosts.length / POSTS_PER_PAGE));

// Redirect logic remains the same
if (Number.isNaN(CURRENT_PAGE) || CURRENT_PAGE < 1) { return Astro.redirect(blogRoot); }
if (CURRENT_PAGE === 1) { return Astro.redirect(blogRoot); }
if (CURRENT_PAGE > totalPages && totalPages > 0) { return Astro.redirect(blogRoot + `page/${totalPages}/`); }

const start = (CURRENT_PAGE - 1) * POSTS_PER_PAGE;
const pagePosts = allPosts.slice(start, start + POSTS_PER_PAGE);

const canonical = new URL(blogRoot + `page/${CURRENT_PAGE}/`, Astro.site).toString();
const prevUrl = CURRENT_PAGE > 1 ? new URL(CURRENT_PAGE === 2 ? blogRoot : blogRoot + `page/${CURRENT_PAGE - 1}/`, Astro.site).toString() : undefined;
const nextUrl = CURRENT_PAGE < totalPages ? new URL(blogRoot + `page/${CURRENT_PAGE + 1}/`, Astro.site).toString() : undefined;

const pageTitle = t('blogPaginated.title').replace('{currentPage}', String(CURRENT_PAGE));
const pageDescription = t('blogPaginated.description');
const h1 = t('blogPaginated.h1');
const firstPageText = t('blogPaginated.firstPage');

const formatDate = (date: string) => new Date(date).toLocaleDateString('hi-IN', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const toAbsolute = (p?: string) => !p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : new URL(p, API_BASE_URL).toString());
---
<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDescription} canonical={canonical} prevUrl={prevUrl} nextUrl={nextUrl} lang={locale}>

  <div class="desktop-layout">
    <Header lang={locale} />
  </div>
  <div class="mobile-layout">
    <MobileAppShell title={`${h1} - पृष्ठ ${CURRENT_PAGE}`} active="blog" lang={locale} />
  </div>

  <main class="blog-index">
    <div class="container">
      <header class="section-head">
        <div>
          <h1>{h1}</h1>
          <p class="muted">{t('blogIndex.pager.pageStatus').replace('{currentPage}', String(CURRENT_PAGE)).replace('{totalPages}', String(totalPages))}</p>
        </div>
        <a href={blogRoot} class="btn-view-all" aria-label="Go to page 1">{firstPageText}</a>
      </header>

      {pagePosts.length === 0 ? ( <p class="muted">{t('blogPaginated.noPosts')}</p> ) : (
        <div class="post-grid">
          {pagePosts.map(async (post) => {
            const postUrl = blogRoot + `${post.slug}/`;
            return (
              <article class="post-card">
                <a href={postUrl} class="card-image-link" aria-label={`Read more: ${post.title}`}>
                  <img src={toAbsolute(post.image)} alt={`Featured image for ${post.title}`} loading="lazy" width="400" height="250" class="card-image"/>
                </a>
                <div class="card-content">
                  <p class="card-meta"><time datetime={post.publishedAt}>{formatDate(post.publishedAt)}</time></p>
                  <h2 class="card-title"><a href={postUrl}>{post.title}</a></h2>
                  <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(post.excerpt || '')} />
                </div>
              </article>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      )}

      <nav class="pager" aria-label="Pagination">
        <ul>
          <li class="desktop-layout"><a class="pg-btn" href={blogRoot} aria-label="Go to first page">« {firstPageText}</a></li>
          <li>{prevUrl ? (<a class="pg-btn" href={prevUrl} aria-label="Previous page">{t('blogIndex.pager.prev')}</a>) : (<span class="pg-btn" aria-disabled="true">{t('blogIndex.pager.prev')}</span>)}</li>
          <li class="pg-status" aria-current="page">{t('blogIndex.pager.pageStatus').replace('{currentPage}', String(CURRENT_PAGE)).replace('{totalPages}', String(totalPages))}</li>
          <li>{nextUrl ? (<a class="pg-btn" href={nextUrl} aria-label="Next page">{t('blogIndex.pager.next')}</a>) : (<span class="pg-btn" aria-disabled="true">{t('blogIndex.pager.next')}</span>)}</li>
          <li class="desktop-layout">{CURRENT_PAGE < totalPages ? (<a class="pg-btn" href={blogRoot + `page/${totalPages}/`} aria-label="Go to last page">{t('blogIndex.pager.last')}</a>) : (<span class="pg-btn" aria-disabled="true">{t('blogIndex.pager.last')}</span>)}</li>
        </ul>
      </nav>
    </div>
  </main>

  <Footer lang={locale} />
</Base>

// ===== src/pages/hi/blog/tag/[tag].astro =====

---
// ===== src/pages/hi/blog/tag/[tag].astro =====
// --- CORRECTED: Now parses Markdown in excerpts ---
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../../../components/Footer.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { getBlogPosts } from '../../../../services/api';
import type { BlogPostListItem } from '../../../../services/api';
import { slugify } from '../../../../lib/paths';

// This is an SSR page, getStaticPaths is removed.

const locale: 'hi' = 'hi';
const { tag: tagSlug } = Astro.params;

const allPosts = await getBlogPosts(locale);

const filteredPosts = allPosts.filter(post => 
  post.tags.map(t => slugify(t)).includes(tagSlug!)
);

const tagName = filteredPosts.length > 0 
  ? filteredPosts[0].tags.find(t => slugify(t) === tagSlug) || tagSlug
  : tagSlug;

const pageTitle = `"${tagName}" टैग की गईं पोस्ट | Starsuu7 ब्लॉग`;
const pageDescription = `Starsuu7 ब्लॉग पर "${tagName}" टैग किए गए सभी ब्लॉग पोस्ट और लेख खोजें।`;
const h1 = `टैग: ${tagName}`;
const canonical = new URL(`/hi/blog/tag/${tagSlug}/`, Astro.site).toString();

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const toAbsolute = (p?: string) => !p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : new URL(p, API_BASE_URL).toString());
const formatDate = (date: string) => new Date(date).toLocaleDateString('hi-IN', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
---
<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDescription} canonical={canonical} lang={locale}>

  <div class="desktop-layout"><Header lang={locale} /></div>
  <div class="mobile-layout"><MobileAppShell title={h1} active="blog" lang={locale} showBack={true} /></div>

  <main class="blog-archive-page">
    <div class="container">
      <header class="page-header">
        <p class="archive-type">ब्लॉग आर्काइव</p>
        <h1>{h1}</h1>
      </header>

      {filteredPosts.length > 0 ? (
        <div class="post-grid">
          {filteredPosts.map(async (post: BlogPostListItem) => {
            const postUrl = `/hi/blog/${post.slug}/`;
            return (
              <article class="post-card">
                <a href={postUrl} class="card-image-link" aria-label={`पढ़ें: ${post.title}`}>
                  <img src={toAbsolute(post.image)} alt={`के लिए विशेष रुप से प्रदर्शित छवि ${post.title}`} loading="lazy" width="400" height="250" class="card-image" />
                </a>
                <div class="card-content">
                  <p class="card-meta"><time datetime={post.publishedAt}>{formatDate(post.publishedAt)}</time></p>
                  <h2 class="card-title"><a href={postUrl}>{post.title}</a></h2>
                  <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(post.excerpt || '')} />
                </div>
              </article>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      ) : (
        <p>इस टैग के लिए कोई पोस्ट नहीं मिली।</p>
      )}
    </div>
  </main>
  
  <Footer lang={locale} />
</Base>

  @media (max-width: 767px) { .blog-archive-page { padding-block: 24px; } .mobile-layout + .blog-archive-page { padding-top: 0; } }

// ===== src/pages/hi/blog/[slug].astro =====

---
// ===== src/pages/hi/blog/[slug].astro =====
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../../components/Footer.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import ArticleHead from '../../../components/ArticleHead.astro';
import SocialShare from '../../../components/SocialShare.astro';
import RecentPosts from '../../../components/RecentPosts.astro';
import SidebarPromos from '../../../components/SidebarPromos.astro';
import SidebarCta from '../../../components/SidebarCta.astro';
import TagCloud from '../../../components/TagCloud.astro';
import AuthorBio from '../../../components/AuthorBio.astro';
import CategoriesList from '../../../components/CategoriesList.astro';
import { getBlogPosts, getBlogPostBySlug } from '../../../services/api';
import { useTranslations } from '../../../lib/i18n';
import type { Locale } from '../../../i18n';

// This function generates the static paths for all HINDI blog posts
export async function getStaticPaths() {
  const posts = await getBlogPosts('hi');
  return posts.map(post => ({
    params: { slug: post.slug },
  }));
}

const locale: Locale = 'hi';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

const { slug } = Astro.params;
const post = await getBlogPostBySlug(slug as string, locale);

if (!post) {
  return new Response(null, { status: 404, statusText: 'Not Found' });
}

// Use HINDI content fields from the API response
const postTitle = post.title.hi;
const postExcerpt = post.excerpt.hi;

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const imageUrl = post.image.startsWith('http') ? post.image : `${API_BASE_URL}${post.image}`;
const contentHtml = await marked.parse(post.body.hi);

const pageTitle = t('blogPost.title').replace('{postTitle}', postTitle);
const pageDescription = postExcerpt;
const canonical = new URL(`/hi/blog/${slug}/`, Astro.site).toString();

const articleJsonLd = {
  '@context': 'https://schema.org',
  '@type': 'BlogPosting',
  'mainEntityOfPage': { '@type': 'WebPage', '@id': canonical },
  'headline': postTitle,
  'description': postExcerpt,
  'image': imageUrl,
  'author': { '@type': 'Organization', 'name': post.author },
  'publisher': {
    '@type': 'Organization', 'name': 'Starsuu7',
    'logo': { '@type': 'ImageObject', 'url': new URL('/logo.webp', Astro.site).toString() }
  },
  'datePublished': new Date(post.publishedAt).toISOString()
};
---

<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDescription} canonical={canonical} jsonLd={articleJsonLd} lang={locale}>
  
  <div class="desktop-layout">
    <Header lang={locale} />
    <main class="post-page">
      <div class="container">
        <div class="layout-grid">
          
          <article class="main-content">
            <figure class="featured-image">
              <img src={imageUrl} alt={`Featured image for ${postTitle}`} width="1200" height="600" />
            </figure>
            <ArticleHead
              title={postTitle}
              publishedAt={post.publishedAt}
              author={post.author}
              tags={post.tags}
              lang={locale}
            />
            <div class="prose" set:html={contentHtml} />
            <SocialShare url={canonical} title={postTitle} text={postExcerpt} />
          </article>

          <aside class="sidebar">
            <div class="sidebar-inner">
              <AuthorBio authorName={post.author} lang={locale} />
              <CategoriesList lang={locale} />
              <TagCloud lang={locale} />
              <RecentPosts excludeSlug={slug} lang={locale} />
              <SidebarPromos lang={locale} />
              <SidebarCta lang={locale} />
            </div>
          </aside>
        </div>
      </div>
    </main>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>

  <div class="mobile-layout">
    <MobileAppShell title={t('blogPost.title').replace('{postTitle}', '')} active="blog" showBack={true} lang={locale}>
      <main class="post-page">
        <article class="main-content">
           <figure class="featured-image">
            <img src={imageUrl} alt={`Featured image for ${postTitle}`} width="1200" height="600" />
          </figure>
          <div class="container">
            <ArticleHead
              title={postTitle}
              publishedAt={post.publishedAt}
              author={post.author}
              tags={post.tags}
              lang={locale}
            />
            <div class="prose" set:html={contentHtml} />
            <SocialShare url={canonical} title={postTitle} text={postExcerpt} />
          </div>
        </article>
      </main>
    </MobileAppShell>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>
</Base>

// Explicitly set locale and get translation function
const locale: Locale = 'hi';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

// Use translation function for page metadata and mobile accordion data
const pageTitle = t('faqPage.title');
const pageDescription = t('faqPage.description');
const h1 = t('faqPage.h1');
const mobileIntro = t('faqPage.mobileIntro');

const faqJsonLd = {
  "@context": "https://schema.org",
  "@type": "FAQPage",

    "acceptedAnswer": { "@type": "Answer", "text": a }
  }))

            <p>गेमिंग अनुभव को रोमांचक बनाए रखने के लिए नियमित रूप से नए गेम जोड़े जाते हैं।</p>

            <h3>रम्मी कैसे खेलें</h3>
            <p>रम्मी एक लोकप्रिय कार्ड गेम है जो वैध सेट और अनुक्रम बनाने पर केंद्रित है। खिलाड़ी अपने हाथ को कुशलता से व्यवस्थित करने के लिए कार्ड उठाते और छोड़ते हैं। जीतने की रणनीतियों और गेमप्ले अंतर्दृष्टि के लिए, कार्ड गेम टिप्स पर हमारे ब्लॉग पोस्ट देखें और अपने कौशल में सुधार करें।</p>

// ===== src/pages/hi/promotions/index.astro =====
// --- UPDATED for Server-Side Rendering (SSR) ---

import Base from '../../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../../components/Footer.astro';
import CrossLinkStrip from '../../../components/CrossLinkStrip.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { getPromotions } from '../../../services/api';
import type { Promotion } from '../../../services/api';
import { useTranslations } from '../../../lib/i18n';
import type { Locale } from '../../../i18n';

const locale: Locale = 'hi';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const abs = (p?: string) => (!p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : `${API_BASE_URL}${p}`));

// --- DYNAMIC DATA FETCHING ---
// This now runs on every server request to this page.
const allPromos = await getPromotions(locale);
const promos = allPromos.filter(p => p.imageUrl);

const pageTitle = t('promotionsIndex.title');
const pageDesc = t('promotionsIndex.description');
const h1 = t('promotionsIndex.h1');
const subheading = t('promotionsIndex.subheading');
const canonical = new URL('/hi/promotions/', Astro.site).toString();

const itemList = {
  '@context': 'https://schema.org',
  '@type': 'ItemList',
  name: h1,
  itemListOrder: 'http://schema.org/ItemListOrderAscending',
  numberOfItems: promos.length,
  itemListElement: promos.map((p: Promotion, i: number) => ({
    '@type': 'ListItem',
    position: i + 1,
    url: new URL(`/hi/promotions/${p.slug}/`, Astro.site).toString(),
    name: p.title
  }))
};
---
<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDesc} canonical={canonical} jsonLd={itemList}>

  <div class="desktop-layout">
    <Header lang={locale} />
    <main>
      <section class="promos-index">
        <div class="container">
          <header class="page-head">
            <h1>{h1}</h1>
            <p class="muted" set:html={subheading}></p>
          </header>

          {promos.length > 0 ? (
            <div class="grid">
              {promos.map((p: Promotion) => {
                const href = `/hi/promotions/${p.slug}/`;
                const img = abs(p.imageUrl);
                const badge = p.badgeText || '';
                return (
                  <article class="card">
                    <a href={href} class="artlink" aria-label={`Open promotion ${p.title}`}>
                      {img && <img src={img} alt="" width="480" height="300" loading="lazy" class="cover" />}
                      {badge && <span class="badge">{badge}</span>}
                    </a>
                    <div class="content">
                      <h2 class="title"><a href={href}>{p.title}</a></h2>
                      {p.subtitle && <p class="subtitle">{p.subtitle}</p>}
                      {p.description && <p class="excerpt">{p.description}</p>}
                      <a class="cta" href={href} aria-label={`Learn more: ${p.title}`}>{t('promotionsIndex.learnMore')}</a>
                    </div>
                  </article>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          ) : (
            <p class="muted">{t('promotionsIndex.noPromos')}</p>
          )}
        </div>
      </section>

      <CrossLinkStrip
        lang={locale}
        showReviews
        limitReviews={6}
        titleReviews="संबंधित समीक्षाएं — Starsuu7 (UU7 • 777)"
        matchTerms={['starsuu7','uu7','777','तीन पत्ती','रम्मी','बोनस','ऑफर']}
      />
    </main>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>

  <div class="mobile-layout">
    <MobileAppShell title={h1} active="promos" lang={locale}>
      <main>
        <section class="promos-index">
          <div class="container">
            <header class="page-head">
              <h1>{h1}</h1>
              <p class="muted" set:html={subheading}></p>
            </header>

            {promos.length > 0 ? (
              <div class="grid">
                {promos.map((p: Promotion) => {
                  const href = `/hi/promotions/${p.slug}/`;
                  const img = abs(p.imageUrl);
                  const badge = p.badgeText || '';
                  return (
                    <article class="card">
                      <a href={href} class="artlink" aria-label={`Open promotion ${p.title}`}>
                        {img && <img src={img} alt="" width="480" height="300" loading="lazy" class="cover" />}
                        {badge && <span class="badge">{badge}</span>}
                      </a>
                      <div class="content">
                        <h2 class="title"><a href={href}>{p.title}</a></h2>
                        {p.subtitle && <p class="subtitle">{p.subtitle}</p>}
                        {p.description && <p class="excerpt">{p.description}</p>}
                        <a class="cta" href={href} aria-label={`Learn more: ${p.title}`}>{t('promotionsIndex.learnMore')}</a>
                      </div>
                    </article>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            ) : (
              <p class="muted">{t('promotionsIndex.noPromos')}</p>
            )}
          </div>
        </section>

        <CrossLinkStrip
          lang={locale}
          showReviews
          limitReviews={3}
          titleReviews="संबंधित समीक्षाएं"
          matchTerms={['starsuu7','बोनस']}
        />
      </main>
    </MobileAppShell>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>
</Base>

// ===== src/pages/hi/promotions/[slug].astro =====

---
// ===== src/pages/hi/promotions/[slug].astro =====
// --- UPDATED for Server-Side Rendering (SSR) ---

import Footer from '../../../components/Footer.astro';
import Header from '../../../components/Header.astro';
import Base from '../../../layouts/Base.astro';
import { getPromotions, getReviews } from '../../../services/api';
import MobileAppShell from '../../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { useTranslations } from '../../../lib/i18n';
import type { Locale } from '../../../i18n';

const locale: Locale = 'hi';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

// --- REMOVED getStaticPaths ---
// This makes the page dynamic and resolves the build warning.

const { slug } = Astro.params;

// Fetch data on every request to this page.
const promo = (await getPromotions(locale)).find(p => p.slug === slug);

if (!promo) return new Response(null, { status: 404 });

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const img = (u: string) => u?.startsWith('http') ? u : `${API_BASE_URL}${u}`;

let reviews: any[] = [];
try { reviews = await getReviews(locale); } catch {}

const promoTitle = promo.title;
const promoSubtitle = promo.subtitle;
const promoDescription = promo.description;
const promoBadgeText = promo.badgeText;
const promoCtaText = promo.ctaText;
const promoDetails = promo.details;

const canonical = new URL(`/hi/promotions/${promo.slug}/`, Astro.site).toString();
const title = `${promoTitle} — Starsuu7 प्रमोशन (UU7 • 777)`;
const description = promoSubtitle || promoDescription || 'Starsuu7 (UU7 • 777) प्रमोशन देखें: बोनस, कैशबैक और मौसमी ऑफ़र।';

const relatedReviews = reviews
  .filter(r => {
    const hay = `${r.title} ${r.excerpt} ${r.gameName}`.toLowerCase();
    const keys = [promoTitle, 'starsuu7', 'uu7', '777', 'तीन पत्ती', 'रम्मी'];
    return keys.some(k => hay.includes(k.toLowerCase()));
  })
  .slice(0, 6);

const ldPromotion = {
  '@context': 'https://schema.org',
  '@type': 'Offer',
  name: promoTitle,
  description: promoDescription,
  url: canonical,
  image: img(promo.imageUrl),
  availability: 'https://schema.org/InStock',
  priceCurrency: 'INR',
  seller: { '@type': 'Organization', name: 'Starsuu7' }
};
---
<Base title={title} description={description} canonical={canonical} jsonLd={ldPromotion}>
  
  <div class="desktop-layout">
    <Header lang={locale} />
    <main>
      <section class="promo-hero">
        <div class="container">
          <a href="/hi/promotions/" class="back">{t('promotionPost.backLink')}</a>
          <h1 class="title">{promoTitle}</h1>
          {promoBadgeText && (
            <span class="badge" style={`--badge:${promo.badgeColor || 'var(--brand-orange)'}`}>{promoBadgeText}</span>
          )}
          <p class="sub" set:html={t('promotionPost.subheading')}></p>
          <div class="hero-media">
            <img src={img(promo.imageUrl)} alt={promoTitle} width="1280" height="720" loading="eager" />
          </div>
          <div class="cta-row">
            {promo.ctaLink && (<a href={promo.ctaLink} class="btn">{promoCtaText || t('promotionPost.claimOffer')}</a>)}
            <a href="/hi/#download" class="ghost">{t('promotionPost.downloadApp')}</a>
          </div>
        </div>
      </section>
      <section class="promo-body">
        <div class="container">
          <div class="content">
            {promoSubtitle && <p class="lead">{promoSubtitle}</p>}
            <p>{promoDescription}</p>
            {promoDetails && promoDetails.length > 0 && (
              <div class="details">
                <h2>{t('promotionPost.howToClaim')}</h2>
                <ol>
                  {promoDetails.map((line) => <li>{line}</li>)}
                </ol>
              </div>
            )}
            <aside class="note">
              <strong>{t('promotionPost.noteTitle')}</strong> {t('promotionPost.noteBody')}
            </aside>
          </div>
        </div>
      </section>
      {relatedReviews.length > 0 && (
        <section class="related">
          <div class="container">
            <header class="section-head">
              <h2>{t('promotionPost.relatedTitle')}</h2>
              <p class="muted">{t('promotionPost.relatedDescription')}</p>
            </header>
            <div class="cards">

                  <div class="meta">
                    <span class="pill">★ {r.rating}/5</span>
                    <span class="game">{r.gameName}</span>
                  </div>
                  <h3 class="ctitle">{r.title}</h3>
                  <p class="excerpt">{r.excerpt}</p>
                </a>
              ))}
            </div>
            <div class="cluster-cta">
              <a class="more" href="/hi/reviews/">{t('promotionPost.seeAllReviews')}</a>
            </div>
          </div>
        </section>
      )}
    </main>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>

  <div class="mobile-layout">
    <MobileAppShell title="प्रमोशन" active="promos" showBack={true} lang={locale}>
      <main>
        <section class="promo-hero">
          <div class="container">
            <h1 class="title">{promoTitle}</h1>
            {promoBadgeText && (
              <span class="badge" style={`--badge:${promo.badgeColor || 'var(--brand-orange)'}`}>{promoBadgeText}</span>
            )}
            <p class="sub" set:html={t('promotionPost.subheadingMobile')}></p>
            <div class="hero-media">
              <img src={img(promo.imageUrl)} alt={promoTitle} width="1280" height="720" loading="eager" />
            </div>
            <div class="cta-row">
              {promo.ctaLink && (<a href={promo.ctaLink} class="btn">{promoCtaText || t('promotionPost.claimOffer')}</a>)}
              <a href="/hi/#download" class="ghost">{t('promotionPost.downloadApp')}</a>
            </div>
          </div>
        </section>
        <section class="promo-body">
          <div class="container">
            <div class="content">
              {promoSubtitle && <p class="lead">{promoSubtitle}</p>}
              <p>{promoDescription}</p>

                <div class="details">

                  <ol>
                    {promoDetails.map((line) => <li>{line}</li>)}

// ===== src/pages/hi/reviews/index.astro =====
// --- CORRECTED: Now parses Markdown in excerpts ---
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../../components/Footer.astro';
import CrossLinkStrip from '../../../components/CrossLinkStrip.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { getReviews } from '../../../services/api';
import type { ReviewListItem } from '../../../services/api';
import { useTranslations } from '../../../lib/i18n';
import type { Locale } from '../../../i18n';

const locale: Locale = 'hi';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const abs = (p?: string) => (!p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : `${API_BASE_URL}${p}`));

const allReviews = await getReviews(locale);
const reviewsWithImages = allReviews.filter(r => r.image);

const heroReview = reviewsWithImages.length > 0 ? reviewsWithImages[0] : null;
const otherReviews = reviewsWithImages.slice(1);

const pageTitle = t('reviewsIndex.title');
const pageDesc = t('reviewsIndex.description');
const h1 = t('reviewsIndex.h1');
const subheading = t('reviewsIndex.subheading');
const canonical = new URL('/hi/reviews/', Astro.site).toString();

const stars = (rating: number) => {
  const full = Math.max(0, Math.min(5, Math.round(rating)));
  return '★★★★★☆☆☆☆☆'.slice(5 - full, 10 - full);
};
---
<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDesc} canonical={canonical}>
  
  <div class="desktop-layout">
    <Header lang={locale} />
    <main>
      <section class="reviews-index-page">
        <div class="container">
          <header class="page-head">
            <h1>{h1}</h1>
            <p class="muted" set:html={subheading}></p>
          </header>

          {heroReview && (
            <section class="hero-review-section" aria-labelledby="hero-review-title">
              <article class="hero-card">
                <div class="hero-image-wrapper">
                  <a href={`/hi/reviews/${heroReview.slug}/`} aria-label={`Read review for ${heroReview.title}`}>
                    <img src={abs(heroReview.image)} alt={`Featured image for ${heroReview.title}`} width="1200" height="600" loading="eager" />
                  </a>
                </div>
                <div class="hero-content">
                  <div class="hero-meta">
                    <span class="pill">{heroReview.gameName}</span>
                    <span class="stars" aria-label={`Rating ${Math.round(heroReview.rating)}/5`}>{stars(heroReview.rating ?? 0)}</span>
                  </div>
                  <h2 id="hero-review-title" class="hero-title"><a href={`/hi/reviews/${heroReview.slug}/`}>{heroReview.title}</a></h2>
                  <div class="hero-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(heroReview.excerpt || '')} />
                  <a href={`/hi/reviews/${heroReview.slug}/`} class="hero-cta">{t('reviewsIndex.readMore')} &rarr;</a>
                </div>
              </article>
            </section>
          )}

          {otherReviews.length > 0 ? (
            <div class="grid">
              {otherReviews.map(async (r: ReviewListItem) => {
                const href = `/hi/reviews/${r.slug}/`;
                return (
                  <article class="card">
                    <a href={href} class="artlink" aria-label={`Open review ${r.title}`}>
                      <img src={abs(r.image)} alt={`Image for ${r.title}`} width="480" height="480" loading="lazy" class="cover" />
                      <span class="pill">{r.gameName}</span>
                    </a>
                    <div class="content">
                      <h3 class="title"><a href={href}>{r.title}</a></h3>
                      <div class="meta">
                        <span class="stars" aria-label={`Rating ${Math.round(r.rating)}/5`}>{stars(r.rating ?? 0)}</span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(r.excerpt || '')} />
                    </div>
                  </article>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          ) : !heroReview ? (
            <p class="muted">{t('reviewsIndex.noReviews')}</p>
          ) : null}
        </div>
      </section>

      <CrossLinkStrip
        lang={locale}
        showPromotions
        limitPromotions={6}
        matchTerms={['starsuu7','uu7','777','तीन पत्ती','रम्मी','बोनस','ऑफर']}
      />
    </main>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>

  <div class="mobile-layout">
    <MobileAppShell title={h1} active="faq" lang={locale}>
       <main>
        <section class="reviews-index-page">
          <div class="container">
            <div class="grid">
              {reviewsWithImages.map(async (r: ReviewListItem) => {
                const href = `/hi/reviews/${r.slug}/`;
                return (
                  <article class="card">
                    <a href={href} class="artlink" aria-label={`Open review ${r.title}`}>
                      <img src={abs(r.image)} alt="" width="480" height="480" loading="lazy" class="cover" />
                      <span class="pill">{r.gameName}</span>
                    </a>
                    <div class="content">
                      <h3 class="title"><a href={href}>{r.title}</a></h3>
                      <div class="meta">
                        <span class="stars" aria-label={`Rating ${Math.round(r.rating)}/5`}>{stars(r.rating ?? 0)}</span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(r.excerpt || '')} />
                    </div>
                  </article>
                );
              })}
            </div>
            {reviewsWithImages.length === 0 && <p class="muted">{t('reviewsIndex.noReviews')}</p>}
          </div>
        </section>
      </main>
    </MobileAppShell>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>
</Base>

// ===== src/pages/hi/reviews/[slug].astro =====
// --- UPDATED: Now includes the CommentsSection component ---
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../../components/Footer.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import RecentPosts from '../../../components/RecentPosts.astro';
import SidebarPromos from '../../../components/SidebarPromos.astro';
import SidebarCta from '../../../components/SidebarCta.astro';
import CommentsSection from '../../../components/CommentsSection.astro'; // <-- IMPORT the component
import { getReviewBySlug } from '../../../services/api';
import { useTranslations } from '../../../lib/i18n';
import type { Locale } from '../../../i18n';

const locale: Locale = 'hi';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

const { slug } = Astro.params;
const review = await getReviewBySlug(slug as string, locale);

if (!review) {
  return new Response(null, { status: 404, statusText: 'Not Found' });
}

const ratingPercent = (review.rating / 5) * 100;
const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const imageUrl = review.image.startsWith('http') ? review.image : `${API_BASE_URL}${review.image}`;
const contentHtml = await marked.parse(review.body.hi);

const pageTitle = t('reviewPost.title').replace('{reviewTitle}', review.title.hi);
const pageDescription = t('reviewPost.description').replace('{gameName}', review.gameName);
const canonical = new URL(`/hi/reviews/${slug}/`, Astro.site).toString();
---
<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDescription} canonical={canonical}>

  <div class="desktop-layout">
    <Header lang={locale} />
    <main class="review-page">
      <div class="container">
        <div class="layout-grid">
          
          <article class="main-content">
            <header class="review-header">
              <h1>{review.title.hi}</h1>
              <p class="review-game-name" set:html={t('reviewPost.reviewOf').replace('{gameName}', review.gameName)}></p>
            </header>
            <div class="prose" set:html={contentHtml} />
            
            <!-- ADDED Comments Section for Desktop -->
            <CommentsSection reviewId={review._id} lang={locale} />

          </article>
          
          <aside class="sidebar">
            <div class="sidebar-inner">
              <div class="summary-card">
                <img src={imageUrl} alt={`Cover art for ${review.gameName}`} class="summary-image" />
                <div class="summary-content">
                  <div class="rating-box">
                    <div class="rating-score">{review.rating.toFixed(1)}</div>
                    <div class="rating-stars" aria-label={`Rating: ${review.rating} out of 5 stars`} style={`--rating-percent: ${ratingPercent}%`}></div>
                    <div class="rating-label">{t('reviewPost.ourRating')}</div>
                  </div>
                  <dl class="summary-meta">
                    <div><dt>{t('reviewPost.game')}</dt><dd>{review.gameName}</dd></div>
                    <div><dt>{t('reviewPost.developer')}</dt><dd>{review.developer}</dd></div>
                  </dl>
                  
                  {review.pros?.hi && review.pros.hi.length > 0 && (
                    <div class="pros-cons">
                      <h4>{t('reviewPost.pros')}</h4>
                      <ul>{review.pros.hi.map(pro => <li>{pro}</li>)}</ul>
                    </div>
                  )}
                   {review.cons?.hi && review.cons.hi.length > 0 && (
                    <div class="pros-cons">
                      <h4>{t('reviewPost.cons')}</h4>
                      <ul>{review.cons.hi.map(con => <li>{con}</li>)}</ul>
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
              <RecentPosts lang={locale} />
              <SidebarPromos lang={locale} />
              <SidebarCta lang={locale} />
            </div>
          </aside>
        </div>
      </div>
    </main>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>

  <div class="mobile-layout">
    <MobileAppShell title="गेम समीक्षा" showBack={true} lang={locale}>
      <main class="review-page">
        <div class="container">
          <article class="main-content">
            <header class="review-header">
              <h1>{review.title.hi}</h1>
              <p class="review-game-name" set:html={t('reviewPost.reviewOf').replace('{gameName}', review.gameName)}></p>
            </header>
            <aside class="sidebar">
              <div class="summary-card">
                <img src={imageUrl} alt={`Cover art for ${review.gameName}`} class="summary-image" />
                <div class="summary-content">
                  <div class="rating-box">
                    <div class="rating-score">{review.rating.toFixed(1)}</div>
                    <div class="rating-stars" aria-label={`Rating: ${review.rating} out of 5 stars`} style={`--rating-percent: ${ratingPercent}%`}></div>
                    <div class="rating-label">{t('reviewPost.ourRating')}</div>
                  </div>
                  <dl class="summary-meta">
                    <div><dt>{t('reviewPost.game')}</dt><dd>{review.gameName}</dd></div>
                    <div><dt>{t('reviewPost.developer')}</dt><dd>{review.developer}</dd></div>
                  </dl>
                  {review.pros?.hi && review.pros.hi.length > 0 && (
                    <div class="pros-cons">
                      <h4>{t('reviewPost.pros')}</h4>
                      <ul>{review.pros.hi.map(pro => <li>{pro}</li>)}</ul>
                    </div>
                  )}
                  {review.cons?.hi && review.cons.hi.length > 0 && (
                    <div class="pros-cons">
                      <h4>{t('reviewPost.cons')}</h4>
                      <ul>{review.cons.hi.map(con => <li>{con}</li>)}</ul>
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
            </aside>
            <div class="prose" set:html={contentHtml} />

            <!-- ADDED Comments Section for Mobile -->
            <CommentsSection reviewId={review._id} lang={locale} />

          </article>
        </div>
      </main>
    </MobileAppShell>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>
</Base>

  .desktop-layout { display: none; } .mobile-layout { display: block; } @media (min-width: 768px) { .desktop-layout { display: block; } .mobile-layout { display: none; } } .review-page { padding-block: 48px; // ===== src/pages/promotions/index.astro =====
// --- UPDATED for Server-Side Rendering (SSR) ---

import Base from '../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../components/Footer.astro';
import CrossLinkStrip from '../../components/CrossLinkStrip.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { getPromotions } from '../../services/api';
import type { Promotion } from '../../services/api';
import { useTranslations } from '../../lib/i18n';
import type { Locale } from '../../i18n';

const locale: Locale = 'en';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const abs = (p?: string) => (!p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : `${API_BASE_URL}${p}`));

// --- DYNAMIC DATA FETCHING ---
// This now runs on every server request to this page.
const allPromos = await getPromotions(locale);
const promos = allPromos.filter(p => p.imageUrl);

const pageTitle = t('promotionsIndex.title');
const pageDesc = t('promotionsIndex.description');
const h1 = t('promotionsIndex.h1');
const subheading = t('promotionsIndex.subheading');
const canonical = new URL('/promotions/', Astro.site).toString();

const itemList = {
  '@context': 'https://schema.org',
  '@type': 'ItemList',
  name: h1,
  itemListOrder: 'http://schema.org/ItemListOrderAscending',
  numberOfItems: promos.length,
  itemListElement: promos.map((p: Promotion, i: number) => ({
    '@type': 'ListItem',
    position: i + 1,
    url: new URL(`/promotions/${p.slug}`, Astro.site).toString(),
    name: p.title
  }))
};
---
<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDesc} canonical={canonical} jsonLd={itemList}>

  <div class="desktop-layout">
    <Header lang={locale} />
    <main>
      <section class="promos-index">
        <div class="container">
          <header class="page-head">
            <h1>{h1}</h1>
            <p class="muted" set:html={subheading}></p>
          </header>

          {promos.length > 0 ? (
            <div class="grid">
              {promos.map((p: Promotion) => {
                const href = `/promotions/${p.slug}/`;
                const img = abs(p.imageUrl);
                const badge = p.badgeText || '';
                return (
                  <article class="card">
                    <a href={href} class="artlink" aria-label={`Open promotion ${p.title}`}>
                      {img && <img src={img} alt="" width="480" height="300" loading="lazy" class="cover" />}
                      {badge && <span class="badge">{badge}</span>}
                    </a>
                    <div class="content">
                      <h2 class="title"><a href={href}>{p.title}</a></h2>
                      {p.subtitle && <p class="subtitle">{p.subtitle}</p>}
                      {p.description && <p class="excerpt">{p.description}</p>}
                      <a class="cta" href={href} aria-label={`Learn more: ${p.title}`}>Learn more</a>
                    </div>
                  </article>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          ) : (
            <p class="muted">{t('promotionsIndex.noPromos')}</p>
          )}
        </div>
      </section>

      <CrossLinkStrip
        lang={locale}
        showReviews
        limitReviews={6}
        titleReviews="Related Reviews — Starsuu7 (UU7 • 777)"
        matchTerms={['starsuu7','uu7','777','teen patti','rummy','bonus','offer']}
      />
    </main>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>

  <div class="mobile-layout">
    <MobileAppShell title={h1} active="promos" lang={locale}>
      <main>
        <section class="promos-index">
          <div class="container">
            <header class="page-head">
              <h1>{h1}</h1>
              <p class="muted" set:html={subheading}></p>
            </header>

            {promos.length > 0 ? (
              <div class="grid">
                {promos.map((p: Promotion) => {
                  const href = `/promotions/${p.slug}/`;
                  const img = abs(p.imageUrl);
                  const badge = p.badgeText || '';
                  return (
                    <article class="card">
                      <a href={href} class="artlink" aria-label={`Open promotion ${p.title}`}>
                        {img && <img src={img} alt="" width="480" height="300" loading="lazy" class="cover" />}
                        {badge && <span class="badge">{badge}</span>}
                      </a>
                      <div class="content">
                        <h2 class="title"><a href={href}>{p.title}</a></h2>
                        {p.subtitle && <p class="subtitle">{p.subtitle}</p>}
                        {p.description && <p class="excerpt">{p.description}</p>}
                        <a class="cta" href={href} aria-label={`Learn more: ${p.title}`}>Learn more</a>
                      </div>
                    </article>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            ) : (
              <p class="muted">{t('promotionsIndex.noPromos')}</p>
            )}
          </div>
        </section>

        <CrossLinkStrip
          lang={locale}
          showReviews
          limitReviews={3}
          titleReviews="Related Reviews"
          matchTerms={['starsuu7','bonus']}
        />
      </main>
    </MobileAppShell>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>
</Base>
