  .desktop-layout { display: none; } .mobile-layout { display: block; } @media (min-width: 768px) { .desktop-layout { display: block; } .mobile-layout { display: none; } } .promos-index { padding-block: 32px 40px; background: var(--surface); border-top: 1px solid var(--ring); } @media (max-width: 767px) { .promos-index { padding-block: 24px; border-top: none; } } .page-head { max-width: 760px; margin: 0 auto 20px; text-align: center; } .page-head h1 { margin: 0 0 8px; font-size: clamp(26px, 4.2vw, 38px); } .grid { display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(280px, 1fr)); gap: 16px; } .card { background: var(--surface-2); border: 1px solid var(--ring); border-radius: 16px; overflow: hidden; display: flex; flex-direction: column; box-shadow: var(--shadow-md); transition: transform .2s ease-out, box-shadow .2s ease-out; } .card:hover { transform: translateY(-4px); box-shadow: var(--shadow-lg); } .artlink { position: relative; display: block; } .cover { width: 100%; aspect-ratio: 16/9; object-fit: cover; display: block; } .badge { position: absolute; left: 10px; top: 10px; padding: 2px 8px; border-radius: 999px; font-size: 12px; font-weight: 900; background: var(--brand-gold); color: #0b0b0f; border: 1px solid color-mix(in oklab, #000 15%, var(--brand-gold)); } .content { padding: 14px; display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 6px; flex-grow: 1; } .title { margin: 0; font-size: 18px; } .title a { color: var(--text-primary); text-decoration: none; font-weight: 800; } .title a:hover { color: var(--brand-orange); } .subtitle { margin: 0; color: var(--text-primary); font-weight: 600; font-size: 13px; } .excerpt { margin: 0; color: var(--text-secondary); font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.55; flex-grow: 1; } .cta { align-self: flex-start; color: var(--brand-orange); font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; } .cta:hover { text-decoration: underline; }

// ===== src/pages/promotions/[slug].astro =====

---
// ===== src/pages/promotions/[slug].astro =====
// --- UPDATED for Server-Side Rendering (SSR) ---

import Footer from '../../components/Footer.astro';
import Header from '../../components/Header.astro';
import Base from '../../layouts/Base.astro';
import { getPromotions, getReviews } from '../../services/api';
import MobileAppShell from '../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { useTranslations } from '../../lib/i18n';
import type { Locale } from '../../i18n';

const locale: Locale = 'en';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

// --- REMOVED getStaticPaths ---
// This function is removed to make the page dynamic (SSR).
// The build warning will now be gone.

const { slug } = Astro.params;

// This code now runs on the server for every request to this page.
const promo = (await getPromotions(locale)).find(p => p.slug === slug);

if (!promo) {
    return new Response(null, { status: 404, statusText: 'Not Found' });
}

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const img = (u: string) => u?.startsWith('http') ? u : `${API_BASE_URL}${u}`;

let reviews: any[] = [];
try { reviews = await getReviews(locale); } catch {}

const promoTitle = promo.title;
const promoSubtitle = promo.subtitle;
const promoDescription = promo.description;
const promoBadgeText = promo.badgeText;
const promoCtaText = promo.ctaText;
const promoDetails = promo.details;

const canonical = new URL(`/promotions/${promo.slug}/`, Astro.site).toString();
const title = `${promoTitle} — Starsuu7 Promotions (UU7 • 777)`;
const description = promoSubtitle || promoDescription || 'Explore Starsuu7 (UU7 • 777) promotions: bonuses, cashback and seasonal offers.';

const relatedReviews = reviews
  .filter(r => {
    const hay = `${r.title} ${r.excerpt} ${r.gameName}`.toLowerCase();
    const keys = [promoTitle, 'starsuu7', 'uu7', '777'];
    return keys.some(k => hay.includes(k.toLowerCase()));
  })
  .slice(0, 6);

const ldPromotion = {
  '@context': 'https://schema.org',
  '@type': 'Offer',
  name: promoTitle,
  description: promoDescription,
  url: canonical,
  image: img(promo.imageUrl),
  availability: 'https://schema.org/InStock',
  priceCurrency: 'INR',
  seller: { '@type': 'Organization', name: 'Starsuu7' }
};
---
<Base title={title} description={description} canonical={canonical} jsonLd={ldPromotion}>
  
  <div class="desktop-layout">
    <Header lang={locale} />
    <main>
      <section class="promo-hero">
        <div class="container">
          <a href="/promotions/" class="back">{t('promotionPost.backLink')}</a>
          <h1 class="title">{promoTitle}</h1>
          {promoBadgeText && (
            <span class="badge" style={`--badge:${promo.badgeColor || 'var(--brand-orange)'}`}>{promoBadgeText}</span>
          )}
          <p class="sub" set:html={t('promotionPost.subheading')}></p>
          <div class="hero-media">
            <img src={img(promo.imageUrl)} alt={promoTitle} width="1280" height="720" loading="eager" />
          </div>
          <div class="cta-row">
            {promo.ctaLink && (<a href={promo.ctaLink} class="btn">{promoCtaText || t('promotionPost.claimOffer')}</a>)}
            <a href="/#download" class="ghost">{t('promotionPost.downloadApp')}</a>
          </div>
        </div>
      </section>
      <section class="promo-body">
        <div class="container">
          <div class="content">
            {promoSubtitle && <p class="lead">{promoSubtitle}</p>}
            <p>{promoDescription}</p>
            {promoDetails && promoDetails.length > 0 && (
              <div class="details">
                <h2>{t('promotionPost.howToClaim')}</h2>
                <ol>
                  {promoDetails.map((line) => <li>{line}</li>)}
                </ol>
              </div>
            )}
            <aside class="note">
              <strong>{t('promotionPost.noteTitle')}</strong> {t('promotionPost.noteBody')}
            </aside>
          </div>
        </div>
      </section>
      {relatedReviews.length > 0 && (
        <section class="related">
          <div class="container">
            <header class="section-head">
              <h2>{t('promotionPost.relatedTitle')}</h2>
              <p class="muted">{t('promotionPost.relatedDescription')}</p>
            </header>
            <div class="cards">
              {relatedReviews.map((r) => (
                <a class="card" href={`/reviews/${r.slug}/`}>
                  <img class="thumb" src={img(r.image)} alt={r.title} width="420" height="260" loading="lazy" />
                  <div class="meta">
                    <span class="pill">★ {r.rating}/5</span>
                    <span class="game">{r.gameName}</span>
                  </div>
                  <h3 class="ctitle">{r.title}</h3>
                  <p class="excerpt">{r.excerpt}</p>
                </a>
              ))}
            </div>
            <div class="cluster-cta">
              <a class="more" href="/reviews/">{t('promotionPost.seeAllReviews')}</a>
            </div>
          </div>
        </section>
      )}
    </main>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>

  <div class="mobile-layout">
    <MobileAppShell title="Promotion" active="promos" showBack={true} lang={locale}>
      <main>
        <section class="promo-hero">
          <div class="container">
            <h1 class="title">{promoTitle}</h1>
            {promoBadgeText && (
              <span class="badge" style={`--badge:${promo.badgeColor || 'var(--brand-orange)'}`}>{promoBadgeText}</span>
            )}
            <p class="sub" set:html={t('promotionPost.subheadingMobile')}></p>
            <div class="hero-media">
              <img src={img(promo.imageUrl)} alt={promoTitle} width="1280" height="720" loading="eager" />
            </div>
            <div class="cta-row">
              {promo.ctaLink && (<a href={promo.ctaLink} class="btn">{promoCtaText || t('promotionPost.claimOffer')}</a>)}
              <a href="/#download" class="ghost">{t('promotionPost.downloadApp')}</a>
            </div>
          </div>
        </section>
        <section class="promo-body">
          <div class="container">
            <div class="content">
              {promoSubtitle && <p class="lead">{promoSubtitle}</p>}
              <p>{promoDescription}</p>
              {promoDetails && promoDetails.length > 0 && (
                <div class="details">
                  <h2>{t('promotionPost.howToClaim')}</h2>
                  <ol>
                    {promoDetails.map((line) => <li>{line}</li>)}
                  </ol>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        </section>
      </main>
    </MobileAppShell>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>

// ===== src/pages/reviews/index.astro =====
// --- CORRECTED: Now parses Markdown in excerpts ---
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../components/Footer.astro';
import CrossLinkStrip from '../../components/CrossLinkStrip.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import { getReviews } from '../../services/api';
import type { ReviewListItem } from '../../services/api';
import { useTranslations } from '../../lib/i18n';
import type { Locale } from '../../i18n';

const locale: Locale = 'en';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const abs = (p?: string) => (!p ? '' : (p.startsWith('http') ? p : `${API_BASE_URL}${p}`));

const allReviews = await getReviews(locale);
const reviewsWithImages = allReviews.filter(r => r.image);

const heroReview = reviewsWithImages.length > 0 ? reviewsWithImages[0] : null;
const otherReviews = reviewsWithImages.slice(1);

const pageTitle = t('reviewsIndex.title');
const pageDesc = t('reviewsIndex.description');
const h1 = t('reviewsIndex.h1');
const subheading = t('reviewsIndex.subheading');
const canonical = new URL('/reviews/', Astro.site).toString();

const stars = (rating: number) => {
  const full = Math.max(0, Math.min(5, Math.round(rating)));
  return '★★★★★☆☆☆☆☆'.slice(5 - full, 10 - full);
};
---
<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDesc} canonical={canonical}>
  
  <div class="desktop-layout">
    <Header lang={locale} />
    <main>
      <section class="reviews-index-page">
        <div class="container">
          <header class="page-head">
            <h1>{h1}</h1>
            <p class="muted" set:html={subheading}></p>
          </header>

          {heroReview && (
            <section class="hero-review-section" aria-labelledby="hero-review-title">
              <article class="hero-card">
                <div class="hero-image-wrapper">
                  <a href={`/reviews/${heroReview.slug}/`} aria-label={`Read review for ${heroReview.title}`}>
                    <img src={abs(heroReview.image)} alt={`Featured image for ${heroReview.title}`} width="1200" height="600" loading="eager" />
                  </a>
                </div>
                <div class="hero-content">
                  <div class="hero-meta">
                    <span class="pill">{heroReview.gameName}</span>
                    <span class="stars" aria-label={`Rating ${Math.round(heroReview.rating)}/5`}>{stars(heroReview.rating ?? 0)}</span>
                  </div>
                  <h2 id="hero-review-title" class="hero-title"><a href={`/reviews/${heroReview.slug}/`}>{heroReview.title}</a></h2>
                  <div class="hero-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(heroReview.excerpt || '')} />
                  <a href={`/reviews/${heroReview.slug}/`} class="hero-cta">{t('reviewsIndex.readMore')} &rarr;</a>
                </div>
              </article>
            </section>
          )}

          {otherReviews.length > 0 ? (
            <div class="grid">
              {otherReviews.map(async (r: ReviewListItem) => {
                const href = `/reviews/${r.slug}/`;
                return (
                  <article class="card">
                    <a href={href} class="artlink" aria-label={`Open review ${r.title}`}>
                      <img src={abs(r.image)} alt={`Image for ${r.title}`} width="480" height="480" loading="lazy" class="cover" />
                      <span class="pill">{r.gameName}</span>
                    </a>
                    <div class="content">
                      <h3 class="title"><a href={href}>{r.title}</a></h3>
                      <div class="meta">
                        <span class="stars" aria-label={`Rating ${Math.round(r.rating)}/5`}>{stars(r.rating ?? 0)}</span>
                      </div>
                       {/* This was missing before, causing the mobile layout to not have excerpts */}
                      <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(r.excerpt || '')} />
                    </div>
                  </article>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          ) : !heroReview ? (
            <p class="muted">{t('reviewsIndex.noReviews')}</p>
          ) : null}
        </div>
      </section>

      <CrossLinkStrip
        lang={locale}
        showPromotions
        limitPromotions={6}
        matchTerms={['starsuu7','uu7','777','teen patti','rummy','bonus','offer']}
      />
    </main>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>

  <div class="mobile-layout">
    <MobileAppShell title={h1} active="faq" lang={locale}>
       <main>
        <section class="reviews-index-page">
          <div class="container">
            <div class="grid">
              {reviewsWithImages.map(async (r: ReviewListItem) => {
                const href = `/reviews/${r.slug}/`;
                return (
                  <article class="card">
                    <a href={href} class="artlink" aria-label={`Open review ${r.title}`}>
                      <img src={abs(r.image)} alt="" width="480" height="480" loading="lazy" class="cover" />
                      <span class="pill">{r.gameName}</span>
                    </a>
                    <div class="content">
                      <h3 class="title"><a href={href}>{r.title}</a></h3>
                      <div class="meta">
                        <span class="stars" aria-label={`Rating ${Math.round(r.rating)}/5`}>{stars(r.rating ?? 0)}</span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="card-excerpt prose-excerpt" set:html={await marked.parse(r.excerpt || '')} />
                    </div>
                  </article>
                );
              })}
            </div>
            {reviewsWithImages.length === 0 && <p class="muted">{t('reviewsIndex.noReviews')}</p>}
          </div>
        </section>
      </main>
    </MobileAppShell>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>
</Base>

// ===== src/pages/reviews/[slug].astro =====
// --- REFACTORED: Now uses the modern two-column layout with a sidebar AND includes the new CommentsSection ---
import { marked } from 'marked';
import Base from '../../layouts/Base.astro';
import Header from '../../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../../components/Footer.astro';
import MobileAppShell from '../../components/MobileAppShell.astro';
import RecentPosts from '../../components/RecentPosts.astro';
import SidebarPromos from '../../components/SidebarPromos.astro';
import SidebarCta from '../../components/SidebarCta.astro';
import CommentsSection from '../../components/CommentsSection.astro'; // <-- IMPORT the new component
import { getReviewBySlug } from '../../services/api';
import { useTranslations } from '../../lib/i18n';
import type { Locale } from '../../i18n';

const locale: Locale = 'en';
const t = useTranslations(locale);

const { slug } = Astro.params;
const review = await getReviewBySlug(slug as string, locale);

if (!review) {
  return new Response(null, { status: 404, statusText: 'Not Found' });
}

const ratingPercent = (review.rating / 5) * 100;
const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const imageUrl = review.image.startsWith('http') ? review.image : `${API_BASE_URL}${review.image}`;
const contentHtml = await marked.parse(review.body.en);

const pageTitle = t('reviewPost.title').replace('{reviewTitle}', review.title.en);
const pageDescription = t('reviewPost.description').replace('{gameName}', review.gameName);
const canonical = new URL(`/reviews/${slug}/`, Astro.site).toString();
---
<Base title={pageTitle} description={pageDescription} canonical={canonical}>

  <div class="desktop-layout">
    <Header lang={locale} />
    <main class="review-page">
      <div class="container">
        <div class="layout-grid">
          
          <article class="main-content">
            <header class="review-header">
              <h1>{review.title.en}</h1>
              <p class="review-game-name" set:html={t('reviewPost.reviewOf').replace('{gameName}', review.gameName)}></p>
            </header>
            <div class="prose" set:html={contentHtml} />
            
            <!-- ADDED Comments Section for Desktop -->
            <CommentsSection reviewId={review._id} />

          </article>
          
          <aside class="sidebar">
            <div class="sidebar-inner">
              <div class="summary-card">
                <img src={imageUrl} alt={`Cover art for ${review.gameName}`} class="summary-image" />
                <div class="summary-content">
                  <div class="rating-box">
                    <div class="rating-score">{review.rating.toFixed(1)}</div>
                    <div class="rating-stars" aria-label={`Rating: ${review.rating} out of 5 stars`} style={`--rating-percent: ${ratingPercent}%`}></div>
                    <div class="rating-label">{t('reviewPost.ourRating')}</div>
                  </div>
                  <dl class="summary-meta">
                    <div><dt>{t('reviewPost.game')}</dt><dd>{review.gameName}</dd></div>
                    <div><dt>{t('reviewPost.developer')}</dt><dd>{review.developer}</dd></div>
                  </dl>
                  
                  {review.pros?.en && review.pros.en.length > 0 && (
                    <div class="pros-cons">
                      <h4>{t('reviewPost.pros')}</h4>
                      <ul>{review.pros.en.map(pro => <li>{pro}</li>)}</ul>
                    </div>
                  )}
                   {review.cons?.en && review.cons.en.length > 0 && (
                    <div class="pros-cons">
                      <h4>{t('reviewPost.cons')}</h4>
                      <ul>{review.cons.en.map(con => <li>{con}</li>)}</ul>
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
              <RecentPosts lang={locale} />
              <SidebarPromos lang={locale} />
              <SidebarCta lang={locale} />
            </div>
          </aside>
        </div>
      </div>
    </main>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>

  <div class="mobile-layout">
    <MobileAppShell title="Game Review" showBack={true} lang={locale}>
      <main class="review-page">
        <div class="container">
          <article class="main-content">
            <header class="review-header">
              <h1>{review.title.en}</h1>
              <p class="review-game-name" set:html={t('reviewPost.reviewOf').replace('{gameName}', review.gameName)}></p>
            </header>
            <aside class="sidebar">
              <div class="summary-card">
                <img src={imageUrl} alt={`Cover art for ${review.gameName}`} class="summary-image" />
                <div class="summary-content">
                  <div class="rating-box">
                    <div class="rating-score">{review.rating.toFixed(1)}</div>
                    <div class="rating-stars" aria-label={`Rating: ${review.rating} out of 5 stars`} style={`--rating-percent: ${ratingPercent}%`}></div>
                    <div class="rating-label">{t('reviewPost.ourRating')}</div>
                  </div>
                  <dl class="summary-meta">
                    <div><dt>{t('reviewPost.game')}</dt><dd>{review.gameName}</dd></div>
                    <div><dt>{t('reviewPost.developer')}</dt><dd>{review.developer}</dd></div>
                  </dl>
                  {review.pros?.en && review.pros.en.length > 0 && (
                    <div class="pros-cons">
                      <h4>{t('reviewPost.pros')}</h4>
                      <ul>{review.pros.en.map(pro => <li>{pro}</li>)}</ul>
                    </div>
                  )}
                  {review.cons?.en && review.cons.en.length > 0 && (
                    <div class="pros-cons">
                      <h4>{t('reviewPost.cons')}</h4>
                      <ul>{review.cons.en.map(con => <li>{con}</li>)}</ul>
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
            </aside>
            <div class="prose" set:html={contentHtml} />

            <!-- ADDED Comments Section for Mobile -->
            <CommentsSection reviewId={review._id} />

          </article>
        </div>
      </main>
    </MobileAppShell>
    <Footer lang={locale} />
  </div>
</Base>

// ===== src/pages/robots.txt.ts =====

// frontend/src/pages/robots.txt.ts
// Dynamic robots.txt (SSR endpoint) for Astro

import type { APIRoute } from 'astro';

export const GET: APIRoute = async ({ site }) => {
  // In dev, `site` can be undefined. Use relative path fallback.
  const siteUrl = (site?.toString() ?? '').replace(/\/$/, '');
  const sitemapIndex = siteUrl ? `${siteUrl}/sitemap-index.xml` : '/sitemap-index.xml';

  const content = [
    'User-agent: *',
    'Allow: /',
    '',
    '# Block internal/admin/API surfaces',
    'Disallow: /api/',
    'Disallow: /adminorg/',
    '',
    '# Primary sitemap index',
    `Sitemap: ${sitemapIndex}`,
  ].join('\n');

  return new Response(content, {
    status: 200,
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'text/plain; charset=utf-8',
      'Cache-Control': 'public, max-age=86400, s-maxage=86400',
    },
  });
};


// ===== src/pages/rss.xml.ts =====

import type { APIRoute } from 'astro';
import { getBlogPosts } from '../services/api';

export const GET: APIRoute = async ({ site }) => {
  const posts = await getBlogPosts();

  const siteUrl = site?.toString().replace(/\/$/, '') ?? '';
  const feedUrl = `${siteUrl}/rss.xml`;

  const items = posts.map((p) => {
    const url = `${siteUrl}/blog/${p.slug}`;
    const pub = new Date(p.publishedAt).toUTCString();
    // Basic HTML escape for description
    const desc = (p.excerpt || '').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;');
    return `
      <item>
        <title><![CDATA[${p.title}]]></title>
        <link>${url}</link>
        <guid>${url}</guid>
        <pubDate>${pub}</pubDate>
        <description><![CDATA[${desc}]]></description>
      </item>
    `.trim();
  }).join('\n');

  const xml = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<rss version="2.0">
  <channel>
    <title>Starsuu7 Blog</title>
    <link>${siteUrl}/blog</link>
    <description>Teen Patti & Rummy tips, news, and updates from Starsuu7.</description>
    <language>en-IN</language>
    <atom:link xmlns:atom="http://www.w3.org/2005/Atom" href="${feedUrl}" rel="self" type="application/rss+xml"/>
${items}
  </channel>
</rss>`.trim();

  return new Response(xml, {
    status: 200,
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/rss+xml; charset=utf-8' }
  });
};


// ===== src/pages/sitemap-index.xml.ts =====

// src/pages/sitemap-index.xml.ts
// Sitemap index for Astro (SSR endpoint)

import type { APIRoute } from 'astro';

const SITEMAPS = [
  'sitemap-static.xml',
  'sitemap-posts.xml',
  'sitemap-reviews.xml',
  'sitemap-promotions.xml',
];

export const GET: APIRoute = async ({ site }) => {
  // Ensure a clean base URL with no trailing slash
  const siteUrl = (site?.toString() ?? '').replace(/\/$/, '');

  const nowIso = new Date().toISOString();

  const body = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<sitemapindex xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">
${SITEMAPS
  .map(
    (name) => `  <sitemap>
    <loc>${siteUrl}/${name}</loc>
    <lastmod>${nowIso}</lastmod>
  </sitemap>`
  )
  .join('\n')}
</sitemapindex>`.trim();

  return new Response(body, {
    status: 200,
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/xml; charset=utf-8',
      // Cache 1h; adjust to your deploy/CDN strategy
      'Cache-Control': 'public, max-age=3600, s-maxage=3600',
    },
  });
};


// ===== src/pages/sitemap-posts.xml.ts =====

// ===== frontend/src/pages/sitemap-posts.xml.ts =====
// Encode slugs so all <loc> and alternate href URLs are RFC-compliant.

import type { APIRoute } from 'astro';
import { getBlogPosts } from '../services/api';
import { createPath } from '../lib/paths';
import { locales } from '../i18n';

export const GET: APIRoute = async ({ site }) => {
  const siteUrl = site?.toString().replace(/\/$/, '') ?? '';
  const posts = await getBlogPosts('en');

  const urlEntries = posts
    .map((post) => {
      const encodedSlug = encodeURIComponent((post.slug ?? '').trim());
      const path = `/blog/${encodedSlug}/`;
      const loc = `${siteUrl}${createPath(path, 'en')}`;

      const alternates = locales
        .map(
          (lang) =>
            `<xhtml:link rel="alternate" hreflang="${lang}" href="${siteUrl}${createPath(
              path,
              lang
            )}" />`
        )
        .join('\n    ');

      const lastmod = new Date(post.publishedAt).toISOString();

      return `
  <url>
    <loc>${loc}</loc>
    <lastmod>${lastmod}</lastmod>
    ${alternates}
  </url>`;
    })
    .join('');

  const xml = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9" xmlns:xhtml="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">${urlEntries}
</urlset>`.trim();

  return new Response(xml, {
    status: 200,
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/xml; charset=utf-8',
      'Cache-Control': 'public, max-age=3600, s-maxage=3600',
    },
  });
};


// ===== src/pages/sitemap-promotions.xml.ts =====

// ===== frontend/src/pages/sitemap-promotions.xml.ts =====
// Encode slugs and merge EN + HI so the sitemap isn't empty if promos are locale-only.

import type { APIRoute } from 'astro';
import { getPromotions } from '../services/api';
import { createPath } from '../lib/paths';
import { locales } from '../i18n';

export const GET: APIRoute = async ({ site }) => {
  const siteUrl = site?.toString().replace(/\/$/, '') ?? '';

  // Fetch both locales to avoid an empty sitemap when promos exist only in HI (or EN).
  const [enPromos, hiPromos] = await Promise.all([
    getPromotions('en').catch(() => []),
    getPromotions('hi').catch(() => []),
  ]);

  // De-dupe by slug (prefer EN title when available, but slug is what matters here).
  const bySlug = new Map<string, { slug: string }>();
  for (const p of [...enPromos, ...hiPromos]) {
    if (p?.slug) bySlug.set(p.slug, { slug: p.slug });
  }

  const urlEntries = Array.from(bySlug.values())
    .map(({ slug }) => {
      const encodedSlug = encodeURIComponent(slug.trim());
      const path = `/promotions/${encodedSlug}/`;
      const loc = `${siteUrl}${createPath(path, 'en')}`;

      const alternates = locales
        .map(
          (lang) =>
            `<xhtml:link rel="alternate" hreflang="${lang}" href="${siteUrl}${createPath(
              path,
              lang
            )}" />`
        )
        .join('\n    ');

      // If your API exposes per-promo timestamps, wire them here. For now, we use "now".
      const lastmod = new Date().toISOString();

      return `
  <url>
    <loc>${loc}</loc>
    <lastmod>${lastmod}</lastmod>
    ${alternates}
  </url>`;
    })
    .join('');

  const xml = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9" xmlns:xhtml="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">${urlEntries}
</urlset>`.trim();

  return new Response(xml, {
    status: 200,
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/xml; charset=utf-8',
      'Cache-Control': 'public, max-age=3600, s-maxage=3600',
    },
  });
};


// ===== src/pages/sitemap-reviews.xml.ts =====

// ===== frontend/src/pages/sitemap-reviews.xml.ts =====
// Robust: merges EN+HI reviews, encodes slugs, and never 500s on API hiccups.

import type { APIRoute } from 'astro';
import { getReviews } from '../services/api';
import { createPath } from '../lib/paths';
import { locales } from '../i18n';

export const GET: APIRoute = async ({ site }) => {
  const siteUrl = site?.toString().replace(/\/$/, '') ?? '';

  // Fetch both locales; never throw — fall back to [] so the route still returns 200.
  const [enReviews, hiReviews] = await Promise.all([
    getReviews('en').catch(() => []),
    getReviews('hi').catch(() => []),
  ]);

  // De-dupe by slug in case sets differ across locales.
  const bySlug = new Map<string, { slug: string }>();
  for (const r of [...enReviews, ...hiReviews]) {
    if (r?.slug) bySlug.set(r.slug, { slug: r.slug });
  }

  const urlEntries = Array.from(bySlug.values())
    .map(({ slug }) => {
      const encodedSlug = encodeURIComponent(slug.trim());
      const path = `/reviews/${encodedSlug}/`;
      const loc = `${siteUrl}${createPath(path, 'en')}`;

      const alternates = locales
        .map(
          (lang) =>
            `<xhtml:link rel="alternate" hreflang="${lang}" href="${siteUrl}${createPath(
              path,
              lang
            )}" />`
        )
        .join('\n    ');

      // If you track per-post lastmod, wire it here. Using "now" is acceptable.
      const lastmod = new Date().toISOString();

      return `
  <url>
    <loc>${loc}</loc>
    <lastmod>${lastmod}</lastmod>
    ${alternates}
  </url>`;
    })
    .join('');

  const xml = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9" xmlns:xhtml="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">${urlEntries}
</urlset>`.trim();

  return new Response(xml, {
    status: 200,
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/xml; charset=utf-8',
      'Cache-Control': 'public, max-age=3600, s-maxage=3600',
    },
  });
};


// ===== src/pages/sitemap-static.xml.ts =====

// ===== frontend/src/pages/sitemap-static.xml.ts =====
// --- CORRECTED: Generates valid xhtml:link structure ---

import type { APIRoute } from 'astro';
import { locales } from '../i18n';
import { createPath } from '../lib/paths';

const STATIC_PATHS = [
  '/',
  '/faq/',
  '/promotions/',
  '/reviews/',
  '/blog/',
  '/privacy-policy/',
  '/terms-of-service/',
  '/responsible-gaming/',
];

function generateUrlEntries(siteUrl: string): string {
  return STATIC_PATHS.map(path => {
    // For each static path, create ONE <url> entry.
    // The <loc> will point to the default language (English) version.
    const loc = `${siteUrl}${createPath(path, 'en')}`;

    // Inside this entry, list ALL language versions as alternates.
    const alternates = locales
      .map(lang => 
        `<xhtml:link rel="alternate" hreflang="${lang}" href="${siteUrl}${createPath(path, lang)}" />`
      )
      .join('\n    ');

    return `
  <url>
    <loc>${loc}</loc>
    <lastmod>${new Date().toISOString()}</lastmod>
    ${alternates}
  </url>`;
  }).join('');
}

export const GET: APIRoute = async ({ site }) => {
  const siteUrl = site?.toString().replace(/\/$/, '') ?? '';
  const urlEntries = generateUrlEntries(siteUrl);

  const xml = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9" xmlns:xhtml="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">${urlEntries}
</urlset>`.trim();

  return new Response(xml, {
    status: 200,
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/xml; charset=utf-8', 'Cache-Control': 'public, max-age=86400' }
  });
};

// ===== src/pages/sitemap.xml.ts =====

export function GET() {
  return new Response(null, {
    status: 301,
    headers: { Location: '/sitemap-index.xml' },
  });
}

// ===== src/services/api.ts =====

// ===== src/services/api.ts =====
// --- UPDATED: Added an interface and fetch function for comments ---

// --- Interfaces ---
// (Keep all existing interfaces: Game, Promotion, ReviewListItem, etc.)
export interface Game { _id: string; gameId: string; name: string; category: string; provider: string; image: string; isNew: boolean; isHot: boolean; }
export interface Promotion { _id: string; slug: string; title: string; subtitle?: string; description: string; details?: string[]; imageUrl: string; ctaLink?: string; ctaText?: string; badgeText?: string; badgeColor?: string; }
export interface ReviewListItem { _id: string; slug: string; title: string; excerpt: string; gameName: string; rating: number; image: string; }
export interface Review { _id: string; slug: string; title: { en: string; hi: string }; excerpt: { en: string; hi: string }; body: { en: string; hi: string }; gameName: string; developer: string; rating: number; image: string; pros: { en: string[]; hi: string[] }; cons: { en: string[]; hi: string[] }; isPublished: boolean; metaTitle?: string; metaDescription?: string; }
export interface BlogPostListItem { _id: string; slug: string; title: string; excerpt: string; author: string; image: string; tags: string[]; publishedAt: string; }
export interface BlogPost { _id: string; slug: string; title: { en: string; hi: string }; excerpt: { en: string; hi: string }; body: { en: string; hi: string }; author: string; image: string; tags: string[]; publishedAt: string; }
export interface SiteSettings { siteName: string; logoUrl: string; apkDownloadLink: string; qrCodeImageUrl: string; telegramUrl: string; whatsappUrl: string; instagramUrl: string; facebookUrl: string; youtubeUrl: string; twitterUrl: string; liveChatUrl: string; }

// --- NEW INTERFACE for a single comment ---
export interface Comment {
  _id: string;
  reviewId: string;
  username: string;
  rating: number;
  text: string;
  createdAt: string;
}

// --- Base API Configuration ---
const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL;
const BACKEND_API_KEY = import.meta.env.BACKEND_API_KEY;

// --- Generic Fetch Function (remains the same) ---
async function fetchData<T>(endpoint: string, options: RequestInit = {}): Promise<T> {
    // ... (fetchData implementation is unchanged)
    if (!API_BASE_URL) { throw new Error('API connection failed: The PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL environment variable is not set.'); }
    const url = `${API_BASE_URL}${endpoint}`;
    try {
        const res = await fetch(url, { ...options, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'x-api-key': BACKEND_API_KEY || '', ...(options.headers || {}), }, cache: 'no-cache', });
        if (!res.ok) { const text = await res.text().catch(() => ''); throw new Error(`[API ${res.status}] ${url}${text ? ` → ${text}` : ''}`); }
        return res.json() as Promise<T>;
    } catch (error) {
        let errorMessage = 'An unknown network error occurred.';
        if (error instanceof Error) { errorMessage = error.message; if (error.cause) { console.error('Network Error Cause:', (error.cause as Error).message); } }
        throw new Error(`Network request failed for ${url}. Is the API server running and accessible? Original error: ${errorMessage}`);
    }
}

// --- API Service Functions ---
// (Keep all existing functions: getSettings, getGames, etc.)
export async function getSettings(): Promise<SiteSettings | null> { try { return await fetchData<SiteSettings>('/frontend-api/settings'); } catch (err) { console.warn('Could not fetch site settings, using fallback values.', err); return null; } }
export async function getGames(lang: 'en' | 'hi' = 'en'): Promise<Game[]> { return fetchData<Game[]>(`/frontend-api/games?lang=${lang}`); }
export async function getPromotions(lang: 'en' | 'hi' = 'en'): Promise<Promotion[]> { return fetchData<Promotion[]>(`/frontend-api/promotions?lang=${lang}`); }
export async function getBlogPosts(lang: 'en' | 'hi' = 'en'): Promise<BlogPostListItem[]> { return fetchData<BlogPostListItem[]>(`/frontend-api/blog?lang=${lang}`); }
export async function getBlogPostBySlug(slug: string, lang: 'en' | 'hi' = 'en'): Promise<BlogPost | null> { return fetchData<BlogPost>(`/frontend-api/blog/${encodeURIComponent(slug)}?lang=${lang}`); }
export async function getReviews(lang: 'en' | 'hi' = 'en'): Promise<ReviewListItem[]> { return fetchData<ReviewListItem[]>(`/frontend-api/reviews?lang=${lang}`); }
export async function getReviewBySlug(slug: string, lang: 'en' | 'hi' = 'en'): Promise<Review | null> { return fetchData<Review>(`/frontend-api/reviews/${encodeURIComponent(slug)}?lang=${lang}`); }

// --- NEW FUNCTION to fetch comments ---
export async function getCommentsForReview(reviewId: string): Promise<Comment[]> {
  if (!reviewId) return [];
  // The endpoint for comments is public and does not require the API key.
  // We will call it directly without using the fetchData helper.
  try {
    const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE_URL}/api/frontend/comments/${reviewId}`);
    if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error(`Failed to fetch comments with status: ${res.status}`);
    }
    return res.json();
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(`Failed to fetch comments for review ${reviewId}:`, err);
    return []; // Return an empty array on error to prevent the page from crashing.
  }
}

  color: var(--text-primary);
  width: 100%;
  max-width: 100%;
  overflow-x: clip;             /* NEW: ensure body never creates sideways scroll */
  -webkit-text-size-adjust: 100%;
  text-size-adjust: 100%;
}

/* Media & SVGs should never push layout wider than viewport */
img, video, svg, canvas, iframe {
  max-width: 100%;
  height: auto;
  display: block;
}

/* Ensure long words/urls don’t force overflow on narrow screens */
:where(p, h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6, li, figcaption, small, code, pre) {
  overflow-wrap: anywhere;
  word-break: normal;
}

/* Grid/Flex children default to min-width:0 so content can shrink instead of overflow */
:where(.container, .grid, .bar, .row, .col, .footer-grid, .stats-card) > * {
  min-width: 0;
}

/* ===== Global Typography ===== */
h1,h2,h3,h4,h5,h6 { 
  font-weight: 800; 
  margin: 0; 
  color: var(--text-primary);
}

p { 
  line-height: 1.7; 
  color: var(--text-secondary); 
  margin: 0; 
}

a { 
  color: var(--brand-orange); 
  text-underline-offset: 3px; 
  text-decoration-thickness: 1px;
}
a:hover { 
  color: color-mix(in oklab, var(--brand-orange) 85%, black); 
}

/* Muted helper */
.muted { 
  color: var(--text-secondary); 
}

/* ===== Layout Container ===== */
.container {
  width: 100%;
  max-width: 1200px;
  margin-inline: auto;
  padding-inline: 16px;          /* Tighter default padding on mobile */
}

@media (min-width: 768px) {
  .container {
    padding-inline: 24px;        /* Restore larger gutters on tablet+ */
  }
}

/* Prevent “100vw” background/grads from causing overflow.
   Use .bleed only where intentional full-bleed is needed. */
.bleed {
  width: 100vw;
  margin-left: calc(50% - 50vw);
  margin-right: calc(50% - 50vw);
  overflow-x: clip;
}

.btn {

}

}

  box-shadow: none;
}

  border-color: var(--ring);
}

/* ===== Sticky CTA Bar: mobile safe area & no overflow ===== */
.sticky-cta-bar {
  position: fixed;
  inset-inline: 0;
  bottom: 0;
  z-index: 1000;
  padding-block: 12px;
  background: var(--surface, #0f1115);
  border-top: 1px solid var(--ring, rgba(255,255,255,.08));
  box-shadow: 0 -4px 15px -3px rgba(0,0,0,0.07);
  transform: translateY(100%);
  animation: slide-up 0.5s 0.5s ease-out forwards;
  display: none;                 /* shown via media query */
  contain: layout paint;         /* isolation prevents expanding page width */
  padding-bottom: max(12px, env(safe-area-inset-bottom)); /* iOS safe-area */
}

@keyframes slide-up { 
  from { transform: translateY(100%);} 
  to { transform: translateY(0%);} 
}

@media (max-width: 767px) { 
  .sticky-cta-bar { display: block; } 
}

.cta-bar-inner { 
  display: flex; 
  justify-content: center; 
  align-items: center; 
}

  will-change: transform;
}

}

/* ===== Common Structural Helpers ===== */

/* Keep headers/sections from leaking gradients/absolutes horizontally */
:where(header, section, footer) {
  overflow-x: clip;
}

/* Make details/summary hit areas not expand width with long content */
details { width: 100%; }
summary { max-width: 100%; }

/* Tables (if ever used) should wrap instead of overflow */
table { width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; }
td, th { min-width: 0; }

/* Buttons/links should never expand past container */
button, .btn, .ghost-btn, .promo-link, .btn-header-download {
  max-width: 100%;
}

/* Defensive: make all grid items respect the grid box (no unintended overflow) */
[class*="grid"] > * { min-width: 0; }

/* Defensive: any absolutely positioned art layers stay clipped to their parent */
.art-wrap, .hero__art { overflow: clip; }
